   169	        if record.evidence_role == "reference" or record.source_type == "reference_profile":
   170	            reference_sources.append(source_ref)
   171	            operator_name = operator_name or _first_non_empty(
   172	                payload.get("operator_name"),
   173	                payload.get("owner"),
   174	            )
   175	            manufacturer = manufacturer or _first_non_empty(payload.get("manufacturer"))
   176	            mission_class = mission_class or _first_non_empty(
   177	                payload.get("purpose"),
   178	                payload.get("mission_class"),
   179	                payload.get("object_type"),
   180	            )
   181	            orbit_regime = orbit_regime or _first_non_empty(
   182	                payload.get("orbit_regime"),
   183	                payload.get("orbit_class"),
   184	            )
   185	            alias_candidates["operator_asset_id"] = alias_candidates.get("operator_asset_id") or _first_non_empty(
   186	                payload.get("operator_asset_id")
   187	            )
   188	            alias_candidates["cospar"] = alias_candidates.get("cospar") or _first_non_empty(
   189	                payload.get("cospar_id"),
   190	                payload.get("international_designator"),
   191	            )
   192	            alias_candidates["satcat"] = alias_candidates.get("satcat") or _first_non_empty(
   193	                payload.get("satcat_id"),
   194	                payload.get("norad_id"),
   195	            )
   196	            alias_candidates["manufacturer_designation"] = alias_candidates.get(
   197	                "manufacturer_designation"
   198	            ) or _first_non_empty(
   199	                payload.get("manufacturer_designation"),
   200	                payload.get("platform"),
   201	            )
   202	            _merge_dimensions(dimensions_json, payload)
   203	
   204	            candidate_verified = _coerce_datetime(record.captured_at) or _coerce_datetime(record.ingested_at)
   205	            if candidate_verified and (last_verified_at is None or candidate_verified > last_verified_at):
   206	                last_verified_at = candidate_verified
   207	        elif record.source_type == "celestrak":
   208	            reference_sources.append(source_ref)
   209	            orbit_regime = orbit_regime or _first_non_empty(
   210	                payload.get("orbital_regime"),
   211	                payload.get("orbit_regime"),
   212	            )
   213	            _merge_dimensions(dimensions_json, payload)
   214	
   215	            candidate_verified = _coerce_datetime(record.captured_at) or _coerce_datetime(record.ingested_at)
   216	            if candidate_verified and (last_verified_at is None or candidate_verified > last_verified_at):
   217	                last_verified_at = candidate_verified
   218	
   219	    normalized_alias_candidates = {
   220	        alias_type: value.strip()
   221	        for alias_type, value in alias_candidates.items()
   222	        if isinstance(value, str) and value.strip()
   223	    }
   224	    reference_sources = _dedupe_strings(reference_sources)
   225	    has_profile_data = any(
   226	        [
   227	            operator_name,
   228	            manufacturer,
   229	            mission_class,
   230	            orbit_regime,
   231	            reference_revision,
   232	            dimensions_json,
   233	            subsystem_baseline_json,
   234	            reference_sources,
   235	            normalized_alias_candidates,
   236	        ]
   237	    )
   238	    return {
   239	        "has_profile_data": has_profile_data,
   240	        "operator_name": operator_name,
   241	        "manufacturer": manufacturer,
   242	        "mission_class": mission_class,
   243	        "orbit_regime": orbit_regime,
   244	        "reference_revision": reference_revision,
   245	        "dimensions_json": dimensions_json,
   246	        "subsystem_baseline_json": subsystem_baseline_json,
   247	        "reference_sources_json": reference_sources,
   248	        "last_verified_at": last_verified_at,
   249	        "alias_candidates": normalized_alias_candidates,
   250	    }
   251	
   252	
   253	async def post_analysis_complete(
   254	    *,
   255	    analysis_id: str,
   256	    session,
   257	    actor_id: str = "system:post-analysis",
   258	) -> None:
   259	    analysis_repo = AnalysisRepository(session)
   260	    asset_repo = AssetRepository(session)
   261	    evidence_repo = EvidenceRepository(session)
   262	    audit_logs = AuditLogRepository(session)
   263	
   264	    analysis = await analysis_repo.get(analysis_id)
   265	    if not analysis:
   266	        return
   267	
   268	    evidence_pairs = await evidence_repo.list_analysis_evidence(analysis_id=analysis.id)
   269	    reference_inputs = _collect_reference_profile_inputs(analysis, evidence_pairs)
   270	
   271	    classification = dict(getattr(analysis, "classification_result", {}) or {})
   272	    baseline_reference = dict(getattr(analysis, "baseline_reference", {}) or {})
   273	    capture_metadata = dict(getattr(analysis, "capture_metadata", {}) or {})
   274	    external_asset_id = (
   275	        baseline_reference.get("external_asset_id")
   276	        or capture_metadata.get("external_asset_id")
   277	        or classification.get("external_asset_id")
   278	    )
   279	    asset_name = (
   280	        baseline_reference.get("asset_name")
   281	        or capture_metadata.get("asset_name")
   282	        or classification.get("name")
   283	    )
   284	
   285	    asset = await asset_repo.resolve_or_create(
   286	        org_id=analysis.org_id,
   287	        norad_id=analysis.norad_id,
   288	        external_asset_id=external_asset_id,
   289	        asset_type=getattr(analysis, "asset_type", "satellite"),
   290	        name=asset_name,
   291	        operator_name=reference_inputs.get("operator_name") or classification.get("operator"),
   292	        alias_candidates=reference_inputs.get("alias_candidates"),
   293	    )
   294	    if getattr(analysis, "asset_id", None) != asset.id:
   295	        await analysis_repo.update_fields(analysis_id, asset_id=asset.id)
   296	        analysis = await analysis_repo.get(analysis_id)
   297	        if not analysis:
   298	            return
   299	
   300	    subsystem = await asset_repo.resolve_or_create_subsystem(
   301	        asset_id=asset.id,
   302	        org_id=analysis.org_id,
   303	        subsystem_key=getattr(analysis, "target_subsystem", None),
   304	        display_name=getattr(analysis, "target_subsystem", None),
   305	        subsystem_type=getattr(analysis, "target_subsystem", None),
   306	    )
   307	    if subsystem and getattr(analysis, "subsystem_id", None) != subsystem.id:
   308	        await analysis_repo.update_fields(analysis_id, subsystem_id=subsystem.id)
   309	        analysis = await analysis_repo.get(analysis_id)
   310	        if not analysis:
   311	            return
   312	
   313	    await asset_repo.update_metadata(
   314	        asset.id,
   315	        norad_id=analysis.norad_id,
   316	        external_asset_id=external_asset_id,
   317	        name=asset.name or asset_name,
   318	        operator_name=(
   319	            asset.operator_name
   320	            or reference_inputs.get("operator_name")
   321	            or classification.get("operator")
   322	        ),
   323	    )
   324	    await evidence_repo.reassign_analysis_evidence(
   325	        analysis_id=analysis.id,
   326	        asset_id=asset.id,
   327	        subsystem_id=subsystem.id if subsystem else None,
   328	    )
   329	    if reference_inputs["has_profile_data"]:
   330	        await evidence_repo.upsert_asset_reference_profile(
   331	            asset_id=asset.id,
   332	            org_id=analysis.org_id,
   333	            operator_name=reference_inputs.get("operator_name"),
   334	            manufacturer=reference_inputs.get("manufacturer"),
   335	            mission_class=reference_inputs.get("mission_class"),
   336	            orbit_regime=reference_inputs.get("orbit_regime"),
   337	            reference_revision=reference_inputs.get("reference_revision"),
   338	            dimensions_json=reference_inputs.get("dimensions_json"),
   339	            subsystem_baseline_json=reference_inputs.get("subsystem_baseline_json"),
   340	            reference_sources_json=reference_inputs.get("reference_sources_json"),

exec

     1	"""
     2	Evidence fusion service — collects and merges evidence from multiple sources.
     3	
     4	Currently supports:
     5	  - Current and historical orbital data from CelesTrak
     6	  - Optional Space-Track SATCAT enrichment when credentials are configured
     7	  - Optional UCS public reference profile ingestion when a text URL is configured
     8	  - Public SatNOGS observation metadata
     9	  - Prior analyses from the database
    10	  - Enhanced space weather snapshots and forecasts from NOAA SWPC
    11	  - ORDEM debris environment data
    12	  - Conjunction screening from CelesTrak SOCRATES
    13	"""
    14	
    15	from __future__ import annotations
    16	
    17	import logging
    18	from datetime import datetime, timezone
    19	
    20	from models.evidence import EvidenceBundle, EvidenceItem, EvidenceSource
    21	
    22	log = logging.getLogger(__name__)
    23	
    24	
    25	async def build_evidence_bundle(
    26	    satellite_id: str = "",
    27	    norad_id: str | None = None,
    28	    org_id: str | None = None,
    29	    include_tle: bool = True,
    30	    include_prior_analyses: bool = True,
    31	    include_weather: bool = True,
    32	    include_debris: bool = True,
    33	    include_conjunction: bool = True,
    34	    include_reference_profile: bool = True,
    35	    include_rf_activity: bool = True,
    36	) -> EvidenceBundle:
    37	    """
    38	    Build a comprehensive evidence bundle for a satellite.
    39	
    40	    Gathers data from all available sources and fuses into a single bundle.
    41	    Each source is independently optional — failure to fetch one doesn't
    42	    block others.
    43	    """
    44	    bundle = EvidenceBundle(
    45	        satellite_id=satellite_id or norad_id or "unknown",
    46	    )
    47	    sat_data: dict | None = None
    48	
    49	    if include_tle and norad_id:
    50	        try:
    51	            from services.celestrak_service import lookup_by_norad_id
    52	            from services.tle_history_service import analyze_tle_history
    53	
    54	            sat_data = await lookup_by_norad_id(norad_id)
    55	            if sat_data:
    56	                bundle.satellite_name = sat_data.get("name", "")
    57	                bundle.add_item(EvidenceItem(
    58	                    source=EvidenceSource.TLE_HISTORY,
    59	                    data_type="application/json",
    60	                    timestamp=sat_data.get("epoch", ""),
    61	                    description=f"Current TLE for NORAD {norad_id}",
    62	                    confidence=0.95,
    63	                    payload={
    64	                        "name": sat_data.get("name"),
    65	                        "altitude_avg_km": sat_data.get("altitude_avg_km"),
    66	                        "inclination_deg": sat_data.get("inclination_deg"),
    67	                        "orbital_regime": sat_data.get("orbital_regime"),
    68	                        "period_min": sat_data.get("period_min"),
    69	                        "eccentricity": sat_data.get("eccentricity"),
    70	                        "country_code": sat_data.get("country_code"),
    71	                        "launch_date": sat_data.get("launch_date"),
    72	                        "rcs_size": sat_data.get("rcs_size"),
    73	                    },
    74	                    metadata={
    75	                        "provider": "CelesTrak",
    76	                        "norad_id": norad_id,
    77	                        "external_ref": f"celestrak:gp:{norad_id}:{sat_data.get('epoch', '')}",
    78	                        "source_url": "https://celestrak.org/NORAD/elements/gp.php",
    79	                        "tags": ["orbital_context", "public"],
    80	                    },
    81	                ))
    82	
    83	            tle_analysis = await analyze_tle_history(norad_id, days=90)
    84	            if tle_analysis.sample_count > 0:
    85	                bundle.add_item(EvidenceItem(
    86	                    source=EvidenceSource.TLE_HISTORY,
    87	                    data_type="application/json",
    88	                    timestamp=tle_analysis.history_end,
    89	                    description=(
    90	                        f"90-day orbital health analysis — "
    91	                        f"{tle_analysis.overall_health_score}/100 ({tle_analysis.health_rating})"
    92	                    ),
    93	                    confidence=0.9 if tle_analysis.sample_count >= 5 else 0.7,
    94	                    payload={
    95	                        "analysis_window_days": tle_analysis.analysis_window_days,
    96	                        "sample_count": tle_analysis.sample_count,
    97	                        "history_start": tle_analysis.history_start,
    98	                        "history_end": tle_analysis.history_end,
    99	                        "altitude_stability_km": tle_analysis.altitude_stability_km,
   100	                        "orbit_decay_rate_km_per_day": tle_analysis.orbit_decay_rate_km_per_day,
   101	                        "eccentricity_stability": tle_analysis.eccentricity_stability,
   102	                        "inclination_drift_deg_per_day": tle_analysis.inclination_drift_deg_per_day,
   103	                        "maneuver_count": tle_analysis.maneuver_count,
   104	                        "maneuver_frequency_90d": tle_analysis.maneuver_frequency_90d,
   105	                        "minimum_altitude_km": tle_analysis.minimum_altitude_km,
   106	                        "maximum_altitude_km": tle_analysis.maximum_altitude_km,
   107	                        "overall_health_score": tle_analysis.overall_health_score,
   108	                        "health_rating": tle_analysis.health_rating,
   109	                        "detected_maneuvers": [
   110	                            {
   111	                                "epoch": event.epoch,
   112	                                "delta_altitude_km": event.delta_altitude_km,
   113	                                "delta_eccentricity": event.delta_eccentricity,
   114	                                "delta_inclination_deg": event.delta_inclination_deg,
   115	                                "estimated_delta_v_m_s": event.estimated_delta_v_m_s,
   116	                                "severity": event.severity,
   117	                            }
   118	                            for event in tle_analysis.detected_maneuvers[:10]
   119	                        ],
   120	                    },
   121	                    metadata={
   122	                        "provider": "CelesTrak",
   123	                        "norad_id": norad_id,
   124	                        "external_ref": f"celestrak:history:{norad_id}:{tle_analysis.history_end}",
   125	                        "source_url": "https://celestrak.org/NORAD/documentation/gp-data-formats.php",
   126	                        "tags": ["orbital_context", "historical", "public"],
   127	                    },
   128	                ))
   129	        except Exception as exc:
   130	            log.warning("TLE evidence fetch failed", extra={"error": str(exc)})

   187	                ]

   335	            description = "Conjunction screening — no recent close approaches found"
   336	            if conjunction.event_count > 0:
   337	                description = (
   338	                    f"Conjunction screening — score {conjunction.conjunction_risk_score}/100, "
   339	                    f"min miss {conjunction.minimum_miss_distance_km:.2f} km"
   340	                )

 succeeded in 0ms:
     1	"""
     2	Insurance Risk Agent — the key differentiator of Orbital Inspect.
     3	
     4	Synthesizes all upstream agent outputs into an actuarial-grade risk assessment
     5	with underwriting recommendation, financial exposure estimates, and consistency
     6	cross-validation. This agent's output is what insurers pay $50K-500K for.
     7	"""
     8	
     9	import logging
    10	from pathlib import Path
    11	from services.gemini_service import (
    12	    is_adk_available,
    13	    run_adk_agent,
    14	    get_model_name,
    15	    parse_json_response,
    16	)
    17	from models.satellite import InsuranceRiskReport
    18	from models.provenance import (
    19	    DataSourceType, ConfidenceCalibration, FinancialEstimate,
    20	    LossProbabilityDerivation, SensitivityAnalysis, FieldProvenance,
    21	)
    22	
    23	log = logging.getLogger(__name__)
    24	
    25	_PROMPT_PATH = Path(__file__).parent.parent / "prompts" / "insurance_risk_prompt.txt"
    26	_PROMPT_TEMPLATE = _PROMPT_PATH.read_text()
    27	
    28	
    29	def _build_agent():
    30	    if not is_adk_available():
    31	        return None
    32	
    33	    from google.adk.agents import Agent
    34	
    35	    return Agent(
    36	        name="insurance_risk_agent",
    37	        model=get_model_name(),
    38	        instruction=_PROMPT_TEMPLATE,
    39	        output_key="insurance_risk_output",
    40	    )
    41	
    42	
    43	_agent = None
    44	
    45	
    46	def _get_agent():
    47	    global _agent
    48	    if _agent is None:
    49	        _agent = _build_agent()
    50	    return _agent

    52	
    53	async def assess_insurance_risk(
    54	    classification_context: str = "",
    55	    vision_context: str = "",
    56	    environment_context: str = "",
    57	    failure_mode_context: str = "",
    58	) -> InsuranceRiskReport:
    59	    """
    60	    Generate an actuarial-grade insurance risk assessment.
    61	
    62	    This is the culminating agent — it receives ALL upstream data and produces
    63	    the underwriting recommendation that insurers act on.
    64	
    65	    Args:
    66	        classification_context: JSON from Classification Agent
    67	        vision_context: JSON from Vision Agent
    68	        environment_context: JSON from Environment Agent
    69	        failure_mode_context: JSON from Failure Mode Agent
    70	
    71	    Returns:
    72	        InsuranceRiskReport with risk matrix, metrics, and underwriting recommendation
    73	    """
    74	    prompt = (
    75	        "Generate a comprehensive insurance risk assessment for this satellite.\n\n"
    76	        f"=== SATELLITE CLASSIFICATION ===\n{classification_context}\n\n"
    77	        f"=== VISUAL DAMAGE ASSESSMENT ===\n{vision_context}\n\n"
    78	        f"=== ORBITAL ENVIRONMENT ===\n{environment_context}\n\n"
    79	        f"=== FAILURE MODE ANALYSIS ===\n{failure_mode_context}\n\n"
    80	        "Provide your complete risk matrix, insurance metrics, and underwriting recommendation."
    81	    )
    82	
    83	    agent = _get_agent()
    84	
    85	    try:
    86	        data = await run_adk_agent(
    87	            agent, prompt
    88	        ) if agent else await _fallback(prompt)
    89	        if "error" in data and "raw_text" in data:
    90	            raise ValueError("Agent response could not be parsed")
    91	
    92	        report = InsuranceRiskReport(**data)
    93	
    94	        # Server-side consistency enforcement
    95	        report = _enforce_consistency(report)
    96	        report = _validate_provenance(report)
    97	        return report
    98	    except Exception as e:
    99	        log.error("Insurance risk assessment failed", exc_info=True)
   100	        return InsuranceRiskReport(
   101	            consistency_check={"passed": False, "anomalies": ["Agent processing error"], "confidence_adjustment": "LOW"},
   102	            risk_matrix={
   103	                "severity": {"score": 3, "reasoning": "Unable to assess — agent error"},
   104	                "probability": {"score": 3, "reasoning": "Unable to assess — agent error"},
   105	                "consequence": {"score": 3, "reasoning": "Unable to assess — agent error"},
   106	                "composite": 27,
   107	            },
   108	            risk_tier="MEDIUM",
   109	            underwriting_recommendation="FURTHER_INVESTIGATION",
   110	            recommendation_rationale="Assessment could not be completed due to a processing error. Manual review required.",
   111	            summary="Automated assessment encountered an error. Recommend manual underwriting review.",
   112	            degraded=True,
   113	        )
   114	
   115	
   116	def _enforce_consistency(report: InsuranceRiskReport) -> InsuranceRiskReport:
   117	    """
   118	    Server-side consistency checks on the insurance risk report.
   119	
   120	    Validates that composite = S×P×C, risk_tier matches composite,
   121	    and recommendation aligns with tier.
   122	    """
   123	    anomalies = list(report.consistency_check.anomalies) if report.consistency_check else []
   124	    rm = report.risk_matrix
   125	
   126	    # Check 1: Composite must equal S × P × C
   127	    expected_composite = rm.severity.score * rm.probability.score * rm.consequence.score
   128	    if rm.composite != expected_composite:
   129	        anomalies.append(
   130	            f"Composite mismatch: reported {rm.composite}, expected {expected_composite} "
   131	            f"({rm.severity.score}×{rm.probability.score}×{rm.consequence.score})"
   132	        )
   133	        rm.composite = expected_composite
   134	
   135	    # Check 2: Risk tier must match composite
   136	    expected_tier = _composite_to_tier(rm.composite)
   137	    if report.risk_tier != expected_tier:
   138	        anomalies.append(f"Tier mismatch: reported {report.risk_tier}, expected {expected_tier} for composite {rm.composite}")
   139	        report.risk_tier = expected_tier
   140	
   141	    # Check 3: Recommendation alignment
   142	    recommendation = report.underwriting_recommendation
   143	    if rm.composite > 80 and recommendation in ("INSURABLE_STANDARD", "INSURABLE_ELEVATED_PREMIUM"):
   144	        anomalies.append(f"Recommendation too lenient: {recommendation} with composite {rm.composite}")
   145	        report.underwriting_recommendation = "UNINSURABLE"
   146	    elif rm.composite <= 15 and recommendation == "UNINSURABLE":
   147	        anomalies.append(f"Recommendation too harsh: UNINSURABLE with composite {rm.composite}")
   148	        report.underwriting_recommendation = "INSURABLE_STANDARD"
   149	
   150	    # Update consistency check
   151	    if report.consistency_check is not None:
   152	        report.consistency_check.passed = len(anomalies) == 0
   153	        report.consistency_check.anomalies = anomalies
   154	        if anomalies:
   155	            report.consistency_check.confidence_adjustment = "Server-side corrections applied"
   156	
   157	    return report
   158	
   159	
   160	def _validate_provenance(report: InsuranceRiskReport) -> InsuranceRiskReport:
   161	    """
   162	    Ensure provenance fields have at least stub values when the LLM omits them.
   163	
   164	    This is the key safety mechanism — reports ALWAYS render, even if the agent
   165	    completely ignores the provenance prompt. Stubs are transparent: they say
   166	    'no attribution provided' rather than fabricating sources.
   167	    """
   168	    if report.confidence_calibration is None:
   169	        report.confidence_calibration = ConfidenceCalibration(
   170	            basis="No structured calibration provided by agent — treat all estimates as approximate",
   171	        )
   172	
   173	    if report.replacement_cost_usd is not None and not report.replacement_cost_detail:
   174	        report.replacement_cost_detail = FinancialEstimate(
   175	            value_usd=report.replacement_cost_usd,
   176	            source="agent_estimate",
   177	            derivation="No structured attribution provided — verify with operator/broker",
   178	        )
   179	
   180	    if report.depreciated_value_usd is not None and not report.depreciated_value_detail:
   181	        report.depreciated_value_detail = FinancialEstimate(
   182	            value_usd=report.depreciated_value_usd,
   183	            source="agent_estimate",
   184	            derivation="No structured attribution provided",
   185	        )
   186	
   187	    if report.revenue_at_risk_annual_usd is not None and not report.revenue_at_risk_detail:
   188	        report.revenue_at_risk_detail = FinancialEstimate(
   189	            value_usd=report.revenue_at_risk_annual_usd,
   190	            source="agent_estimate",
   191	            derivation="No structured attribution provided",
   192	        )
   193	
   194	    if report.total_loss_probability is not None and not report.loss_probability_derivation:
   195	        report.loss_probability_derivation = LossProbabilityDerivation(
   196	            total_loss_probability=report.total_loss_probability,
   197	            derivation_narrative="No structured derivation provided — probability is an agent estimate without explicit base rates",
   198	        )
   199	
   200	    # Stub FieldProvenance for key metrics
   201	    stub_prov = FieldProvenance(
   202	        source_type=DataSourceType.ESTIMATED,
   203	        primary_source="agent_inference",
   204	        caveats=["No structured provenance provided by agent"],
   205	    )
   206	    if report.estimated_remaining_life_years is not None and not report.remaining_life_provenance:
   207	        report.remaining_life_provenance = stub_prov.model_copy()
   208	    if report.power_margin_percentage is not None and not report.power_margin_provenance:
   209	        report.power_margin_provenance = stub_prov.model_copy()
   210	    if report.annual_degradation_rate_pct is not None and not report.degradation_rate_provenance:
   211	        report.degradation_rate_provenance = stub_prov.model_copy()
   212	
   213	    return report
   214	
   215	
   216	def _composite_to_tier(composite: int) -> str:
   217	    if composite <= 15:
   218	        return "LOW"
   219	    if composite <= 35:
   220	        return "MEDIUM"
   221	    if composite <= 60:
   222	        return "MEDIUM-HIGH"
   223	    if composite <= 90:
   224	        return "HIGH"
   225	    return "CRITICAL"
   226	
   227	
   228	async def _fallback(prompt: str) -> dict:
   229	    from services.gemini_service import client, get_model_name as gmn
   230	    from google.genai import types
   231	    import asyncio
   232	
   233	    def _sync():
   234	        return client.models.generate_content(
   235	            model=gmn(),
   236	            contents=types.Content(
   237	                role="user",
   238	                parts=[types.Part.from_text(text=_PROMPT_TEMPLATE + "\n\n" + prompt)],
   239	            ),
   240	            config=types.GenerateContentConfig(
   241	                response_mime_type="application/json",
   242	                temperature=0.1,
   243	            ),
   244	        )
   245	
   246	    loop = asyncio.get_running_loop()
   247	    response = await loop.run_in_executor(None, _sync)
   248	    return parse_json_response(response.text or "{}")

/bin/bash -lc "nl -ba backend/agents/orchestrator.py | sed -n '1,420p'" in /mnt/c/Users/kiran/myprojects/orbital-inspect

     1	"""
     2	Orchestrator — 5-stage satellite inspection pipeline with SSE streaming.
     3	
     4	Runs agents sequentially, streaming SSE events between stages:
     5	  1. Orbital Classification → identify satellite
     6	  2. Satellite Vision → detect damage
     7	  3. Orbital Environment → assess hazards
     8	  4. Failure Mode → determine mechanism + precedents
     9	  5. Insurance Risk → actuarial-grade risk score
    10	
    11	Each agent's output feeds into the next, building a complete
    12	Satellite Condition Report.
    13	"""
    14	
    15	import json
    16	import logging
    17	import uuid
    18	from typing import AsyncGenerator
    19	
    20	from models.events import AgentEvent
    21	from services.resilience import resilient_call, gemini_breaker, CircuitBreakerOpen
    22	from services.sse_service import format_sse_event, format_sse_done, format_sse_error
    23	from config import settings
    24	
    25	log = logging.getLogger(__name__)
    26	
    27	AGENT_ORDER = [
    28	    "orbital_classification",
    29	    "satellite_vision",
    30	    "orbital_environment",
    31	    "failure_mode",
    32	    "insurance_risk",
    33	]
    34	
    35	
    36	def _safe_error(agent: str, exc: Exception) -> str:
    37	    """Log full exception server-side, return safe message for client."""
    38	    err_id = uuid.uuid4().hex[:8]
    39	    log.error("[%s] failed err_id=%s", agent, err_id, exc_info=True)
    40	    return f"Analysis failed (ref: {err_id})"
    41	
    42	
    43	async def run_satellite_pipeline(
    44	    image_bytes: bytes,
    45	    image_mime: str = "image/jpeg",
    46	    norad_id: str | None = None,
    47	    additional_context: str = "",
    48	    analysis_id: str | None = None,
    49	) -> AsyncGenerator[dict, None]:
    50	    """
    51	    Execute the full 5-agent satellite inspection pipeline.
    52	
    53	    Yields SSE-formatted events for each agent stage. The frontend
    54	    consumes these via EventSource to show real-time progress.
    55	    """
    56	    # Generate analysis_id and sequence counter for SSE v2
    57	    analysis_id = analysis_id or uuid.uuid4().hex
    58	    seq = 0
    59	
    60	    if settings.E2E_TEST_MODE:
    61	        from services.e2e_stub_service import run_e2e_stub_pipeline
    62	
    63	        async for event in run_e2e_stub_pipeline(
    64	            analysis_id=analysis_id,
    65	            norad_id=norad_id,
    66	            additional_context=additional_context,
    67	        ):
    68	            yield event
    69	        return
    70	
    71	    def _event(evt: AgentEvent) -> dict:
    72	        nonlocal seq
    73	        evt.analysis_id = analysis_id
    74	        evt.sequence = seq
    75	        seq += 1
    76	        return format_sse_event(evt)
    77	
    78	    # Queue all agents
    79	    for agent_name in AGENT_ORDER:
    80	        yield _event(AgentEvent.queued(agent_name))
    81	
    82	    evidence_gaps: list[str] = []
    83	    degraded_agents: set[str] = set()
    84	
    85	    # ── Stage 1: Orbital Classification ──────────────────────────────
    86	    yield _event(AgentEvent.thinking(
    87	        "orbital_classification", "Identifying satellite type, bus platform, and orbital regime..."
    88	    ))
    89	
    90	    try:
    91	        from agents.orbital_classification_agent import classify_satellite
    92	        classification = await resilient_call(
    93	            lambda: classify_satellite(
    94	                image_bytes=image_bytes,
    95	                image_mime=image_mime,
    96	                norad_id=norad_id,
    97	                additional_context=additional_context,
    98	            ),
    99	            timeout_seconds=settings.AGENT_TIMEOUT_SECONDS,
   100	            max_retries=2,
   101	            circuit_breaker=gemini_breaker,
   102	        )
   103	        classification_dict = classification.model_dump()
   104	        if classification.degraded:
   105	            degraded_agents.add("orbital_classification")
   106	        yield _event(
   107	            AgentEvent.complete(
   108	                "orbital_classification",
   109	                classification_dict,
   110	                degraded=classification.degraded,
   111	            )
   112	        )
   113	    except CircuitBreakerOpen:
   114	        msg = _safe_error("orbital_classification", Exception("Service temporarily unavailable"))
   115	        yield _event(AgentEvent.error("orbital_classification", msg, degraded=True))
   116	        yield format_sse_error("Gemini API circuit breaker is open — service recovering")
   117	        yield format_sse_done("failed")
   118	        return
   119	    except Exception as e:
   120	        msg = _safe_error("orbital_classification", e)
   121	        yield _event(AgentEvent.error("orbital_classification", msg, degraded=True))
   122	        yield format_sse_error("Pipeline failed at satellite classification")
   123	        yield format_sse_done("failed")
   124	        return
   125	
   126	    # Fail-closed: reject non-satellite imagery
   127	    if not classification.valid:
   128	        yield _event(AgentEvent.error(
   129	            "orbital_classification",
   130	            classification.rejection_reason or "Image rejected: not a satellite",
   131	            degraded=True,
   132	        ))
   133	        yield format_sse_done("rejected")
   134	        return
   135	
   136	    # Build satellite context for downstream agents
   137	    sat_context = (
   138	        f"Satellite: {classification.satellite_type}, Bus: {classification.bus_platform or 'unknown'}, "
   139	        f"Regime: {classification.orbital_regime}, Design life: {classification.design_life_years or 'unknown'} years, "
   140	        f"Age: {classification.estimated_age_years or 'unknown'} years, "
   141	        f"Components: {', '.join(classification.expected_components)}"
   142	    )
   143	
   144	    # ── Stage 2: Satellite Vision ────────────────────────────────────
   145	    yield _event(AgentEvent.thinking(
   146	        "satellite_vision", "Scanning for micrometeorite impacts, solar cell degradation, thermal damage..."
   147	    ))
   148	
   149	    try:
   150	        from agents.satellite_vision_agent import analyze_satellite_image
   151	        vision = await resilient_call(
   152	            lambda: analyze_satellite_image(
   153	                image_bytes=image_bytes,
   154	                image_mime=image_mime,
   155	                satellite_context=sat_context,
   156	            ),
   157	            timeout_seconds=settings.AGENT_TIMEOUT_SECONDS,
   158	            max_retries=2,
   159	            circuit_breaker=gemini_breaker,
   160	        )
   161	        vision_dict = vision.model_dump()
   162	        if vision.degraded:
   163	            degraded_agents.add("satellite_vision")
   164	            evidence_gaps.append("satellite_vision")
   165	        yield _event(AgentEvent.complete("satellite_vision", vision_dict, degraded=vision.degraded))
   166	    except Exception as e:
   167	        msg = _safe_error("satellite_vision", e)
   168	        yield _event(AgentEvent.error("satellite_vision", msg, degraded=True))
   169	        vision = None
   170	        vision_dict = {}
   171	        evidence_gaps.append("satellite_vision")
   172	
   173	    # ── Stage 3: Orbital Environment ─────────────────────────────────
   174	    yield _event(AgentEvent.thinking(
   175	        "orbital_environment", "Querying NASA ORDEM debris flux and NOAA space weather..."
   176	    ))
   177	
   178	    # Extract orbital parameters from classification
   179	    altitude_km = None
   180	    inclination_deg = None
   181	
   182	    # Try to get altitude from CelesTrak data if NORAD ID was provided
   183	    if norad_id:
   184	        try:
   185	            from services.celestrak_service import lookup_by_norad_id
   186	            celestrak_data = await lookup_by_norad_id(norad_id)
   187	            if celestrak_data:
   188	                altitude_km = celestrak_data.get("altitude_avg_km")
   189	                inclination_deg = celestrak_data.get("inclination_deg")
   190	        except Exception:
   191	            log.warning("[orchestrator] CelesTrak lookup failed for NORAD %s", norad_id, exc_info=True)
   192	
   193	    try:
   194	        from agents.orbital_environment_agent import analyze_orbital_environment
   195	        environment = await resilient_call(
   196	            lambda: analyze_orbital_environment(
   197	                altitude_km=altitude_km,
   198	                inclination_deg=inclination_deg,
   199	                orbital_regime=classification.orbital_regime,
   200	                satellite_context=sat_context,
   201	            ),
   202	            timeout_seconds=settings.AGENT_TIMEOUT_SECONDS,
   203	            max_retries=2,
   204	            circuit_breaker=gemini_breaker,
   205	        )
   206	        environment_dict = environment.model_dump()
   207	        if environment.degraded:
   208	            degraded_agents.add("orbital_environment")
   209	            evidence_gaps.append("orbital_environment")
   210	        yield _event(
   211	            AgentEvent.complete("orbital_environment", environment_dict, degraded=environment.degraded)
   212	        )
   213	    except Exception as e:
   214	        msg = _safe_error("orbital_environment", e)
   215	        yield _event(AgentEvent.error("orbital_environment", msg, degraded=True))
   216	        environment = None
   217	        environment_dict = {}
   218	        evidence_gaps.append("orbital_environment")
   219	
   220	    # ── Stage 4: Failure Mode Analysis ───────────────────────────────
   221	    yield _event(AgentEvent.thinking(
   222	        "failure_mode", "Analyzing failure mechanisms and matching historical precedents..."
   223	    ))
   224	
   225	    try:
   226	        from agents.satellite_failure_mode_agent import analyze_failure_modes
   227	        failure_mode = await resilient_call(
   228	            lambda: analyze_failure_modes(
   229	                classification_context=json.dumps(classification_dict, default=str),
   230	                vision_context=json.dumps(vision_dict, default=str),
   231	                environment_context=json.dumps(environment_dict, default=str),
   232	            ),
   233	            timeout_seconds=settings.AGENT_TIMEOUT_SECONDS,
   234	            max_retries=2,
   235	            circuit_breaker=gemini_breaker,
   236	        )
   237	        failure_mode_dict = failure_mode.model_dump()
   238	        if failure_mode.degraded:
   239	            degraded_agents.add("failure_mode")
   240	            evidence_gaps.append("failure_mode")
   241	        yield _event(AgentEvent.complete("failure_mode", failure_mode_dict, degraded=failure_mode.degraded))
   242	    except Exception as e:
   243	        msg = _safe_error("failure_mode", e)
   244	        yield _event(AgentEvent.error("failure_mode", msg, degraded=True))
   245	        failure_mode = None
   246	        failure_mode_dict = {}
   247	        evidence_gaps.append("failure_mode")
   248	
   249	    # ── Stage 5: Insurance Risk Assessment ───────────────────────────
   250	    yield _event(AgentEvent.thinking(
   251	        "insurance_risk", "Computing risk matrix, financial exposure, and underwriting recommendation..."
   252	    ))
   253	
   254	    # Build evidence gap context for insurance risk agent
   255	    evidence_gap_context = ""
   256	    if evidence_gaps:
   257	        evidence_gap_context = (
   258	            f"\n\nWARNING — INCOMPLETE EVIDENCE: The following pipeline stages failed and "
   259	            f"their data is missing from this assessment: {', '.join(evidence_gaps)}. "
   260	            f"You must account for this missing evidence in your risk assessment and recommendation."
   261	        )
   262	
   263	    try:
   264	        from agents.insurance_risk_agent import assess_insurance_risk
   265	        insurance_risk = await resilient_call(
   266	            lambda: assess_insurance_risk(
   267	                classification_context=json.dumps(classification_dict, default=str),
   268	                vision_context=json.dumps(vision_dict, default=str),
   269	                environment_context=json.dumps(environment_dict, default=str),
   270	                failure_mode_context=json.dumps(failure_mode_dict, default=str) + evidence_gap_context,
   271	            ),
   272	            timeout_seconds=settings.AGENT_TIMEOUT_SECONDS,
   273	            max_retries=2,
   274	            circuit_breaker=gemini_breaker,
   275	        )
   276	        insurance_risk_dict = insurance_risk.model_dump()
   277	
   278	        # Force partial report metadata when evidence is missing
   279	        if evidence_gaps:
   280	            insurance_risk_dict["evidence_gaps"] = evidence_gaps
   281	            insurance_risk_dict["report_completeness"] = "PARTIAL"
   282	            if insurance_risk_dict.get("underwriting_recommendation") not in ("FURTHER_INVESTIGATION", "UNINSURABLE"):
   283	                insurance_risk_dict["underwriting_recommendation"] = "FURTHER_INVESTIGATION"
   284	                insurance_risk_dict["recommendation_rationale"] = (
   285	                    f"Incomplete evidence: {', '.join(evidence_gaps)} failed. "
   286	                    + insurance_risk_dict.get("recommendation_rationale", "")
   287	                )
   288	        if insurance_risk.degraded:
   289	            degraded_agents.add("insurance_risk")
   290	            insurance_risk_dict["report_completeness"] = "PARTIAL"
   291	        yield _event(
   292	            AgentEvent.complete(
   293	                "insurance_risk",
   294	                insurance_risk_dict,
   295	                degraded=insurance_risk.degraded or bool(evidence_gaps),
   296	            )
   297	        )
   298	    except Exception as e:
   299	        msg = _safe_error("insurance_risk", e)
   300	        yield _event(AgentEvent.error("insurance_risk", msg, degraded=True))
   301	        yield format_sse_done("failed")
   302	        return
   303	
   304	    # ── Pipeline Complete ────────────────────────────────────────────
   305	    terminal_status = "completed_partial" if evidence_gaps or degraded_agents else "completed"
   306	    yield format_sse_done(terminal_status)

   191	    to a runtime analysis — this is the key safety invariant of Phase 5."""
   192	    asset_repo = AssetRepository(session)

/bin/bash -lc "nl -ba ops/architecture/KARPATHY_LLM_WIKI_STRATEGY.md | sed -n '521,820p'" in /mnt/c/Users/kiran/myprojects/orbital-inspect
 succeeded in 0ms:
   521	
   522	### 1. Do not treat markdown as the source of truth
   523	
   524	Karpathy's gist is local-first and markdown-centric because it optimizes for personal knowledge work.
   525	
   526	Orbital Inspect is a governed production system.
   527	
   528	Use markdown pages as inspection artifacts and operator-facing documents, but keep canonical claims and relations in the database.
   529	
   530	### 2. Do not let compiled knowledge bypass provenance
   531	
   532	Every compiled claim must point back to:
   533	
   534	- evidence records
   535	- analysis outputs
   536	- review actions
   537	- source timestamps
   538	
   539	If a claim cannot be traced, it cannot be runtime-eligible.
   540	
   541	### 3. Do not merge tenant and global memory casually
   542	
   543	This repo already has organization boundaries. The compiled layer must have scoping:
   544	
   545	- global public knowledge
   546	- tenant-shared private knowledge
   547	- case-private working memory
   548	- operator-only notes
   549	
   550	### 4. Do not use embeddings as the first answer to every problem
   551	
   552	Orbital Inspect has strong typed structure. Start with:
   553	
   554	- Postgres full-text or BM25-like search
   555	- filters on asset, subsystem, source type, time, orbit regime, classification
   556	- graph traversal
   557	
   558	Add vectors only where semantic recall proves necessary.
   559	
   560	### 5. Do not allow automatic contradiction resolution to change decisions silently
   561	
   562	Contradictions should create:
   563	
   564	- reviewable proposals
   565	- supersession suggestions
   566	- context-pack warnings
   567	
   568	They should not rewrite authoritative case memory without traceable review.
   569	
   570	## Implementation Plan
   571	
   572	### Phase 0: Pick the Thin Slice and Define the Demo
   573	
   574	Time: 1 to 2 days
   575	
   576	Deliverables:
   577	
   578	- choose one agent, one anomaly family or precedent type, and one retrieval question
   579	- define the magic demo in concrete terms
   580	- define what counts as success before any infrastructure build-out
   581	
   582	Recommended starting question:
   583	
   584	- "Can prior insurance-risk precedents improve the next `insurance_risk` synthesis for similar cases?"
   585	
   586	Repo impact:
   587	
   588	- update this architecture note
   589	- add a tiny schema/policy note for the thin slice only
   590	
   591	Success criterion:
   592	
   593	- the team can explain the demo in one paragraph and identify exactly which next-step decision should improve
   594	
   595	### Phase 1: Crystallize Completed Analyses into Inspectable Case Pages
   596	
   597	Time: 3 to 5 days
   598	
   599	Deliverables:
   600	
   601	- on completed analysis, generate one human-inspectable case page
   602	- include compact structured summary data sufficient to power later retrieval
   603	- persist the page and the run metadata
   604	
   605	Repo impact:
   606	
   607	- `backend/db/models.py`
   608	- `backend/db/repository.py`
   609	- new `backend/services/knowledge_crystallizer.py`
   610	- hook from `backend/services/post_analysis_service.py`
   611	
   612	Success criterion:
   613	
   614	- every selected completed analysis yields a case page an analyst can browse and verify
   615	
   616	### Phase 2: Build a Context Pack for One Agent
   617	
   618	Time: 3 to 5 days
   619	
   620	Deliverables:
   621	
   622	- build a compact precedent context pack only for `insurance_risk`
   623	- source it from the new case pages plus existing evidence lineage
   624	- persist the exact pack for audit and replay
   625	
   626	Repo impact:
   627	
   628	- new `backend/services/context_pack_service.py`
   629	- prompt-assembly changes near the `insurance_risk` agent call path
   630	- persistence of context pack summaries for audit
   631	
   632	Success criterion:
   633	
   634	- one new analysis can consume prior compiled case memory in a targeted, inspectable way
   635	
   636	### Phase 3: Prove Uplift Before Expanding Scope
   637	
   638	Time: 2 to 4 days
   639	
   640	Deliverables:
   641	
   642	- offline eval set for precedent retrieval and insurance-risk synthesis
   643	- compare baseline vs context-pack-assisted behavior
   644	- measure token cost, latency, and citation quality
   645	
   646	Repo impact:
   647	
   648	- new tests beside `backend/tests/test_offline_eval.py`
   649	- likely `test_context_pack_service.py`
   650	- likely `test_knowledge_crystallizer.py`
   651	
   652	Success criterion:
   653	
   654	- the thin slice shows measurable improvement or the plan is revised before further platform work
   655	
   656	### Phase 4: Add Canonical Claims and Human Review
   657	
   658	Time: 4 to 6 days
   659	
   660	Deliverables:
   661	
   662	- introduce `knowledge_claims` only after the thin slice works
   663	- add human review states, runtime eligibility, and supersession
   664	- keep case pages as first-class inspectable artifacts
   665	
   666	Repo impact:
   667	
   668	- `backend/db/models.py`
   669	- `backend/db/repository.py`
   670	- new `backend/services/knowledge_service.py`
   671	
   672	Success criterion:
   673	
   674	- compiled memory becomes structured without becoming opaque
   675	
   676	### Phase 5: Add Search and Traversal Only as Needed
   677	
   678	Time: 5 to 8 days
   679	
   680	Deliverables:
   681	
   682	- lexical search over case pages and claims
   683	- graph traversal over typed relations if retrieval quality requires it
   684	- optional vector retrieval behind a feature flag only if evals justify it
   685	
   686	Recommendation:
   687	
   688	- start with Postgres and explicit graph walks
   689	- do not introduce external search infra first
   690	
   691	Success criterion:
   692	
   693	- "find similar cases" becomes reliably useful without creating a disproportionate platform burden
   694	
   695	### Phase 6: Expand to More Agents and Fleet Memory
   696	
   697	Time: 5 to 8 days
   698	
   699	Deliverables:
   700	
   701	- extend context packs to additional agents if they show real benefit
   702	- add asset dossiers, precedent pages, and fleet-memory summaries
   703	- expand contradiction detection, decay, and retention policy
   704	
   705	Special rule:
   706	
   707	- architecture and mission baseline claims decay slowly
   708	- transient anomaly interpretations decay faster
   709	- runtime eligibility expires unless reconfirmed
   710	
   711	Success criterion:
   712	
   713	- the system compounds across agents and fleets without losing inspectability or governance
   714	
   715	### Phase 7: Full Safety Gates
   716	
   717	Time: 3 to 5 days
   718	
   719	Deliverables:
   720	
   721	- tests proving runtime decisions never rely on unreviewed or tenant-incompatible claims
   722	- contradiction handling and decay policy tests
   723	- benchmarks for latency and token usage at expanded scope
   724	
   725	Success criterion:
   726	
   727	- the larger memory layer remains fail-closed and auditable
   728	
   729	## Recommended First 30 Days
   730	
   731	If I were operating as Karpathy-style product architect on this repo, I would do this in order:
   732	
   733	1. pick one agent and one precedent question
   734	2. generate inspectable case pages from completed analyses
   735	3. feed those pages back into one next-step context pack
   736	4. prove uplift with evals before expanding scope
   737	5. only then add canonical claims, review states, and broader retrieval
   738	
   739	This order matters because the product needs one visible compounding loop before it needs a large memory platform.
   740	
   741	## Success Metrics
   742	
   743	Track these from day one:
   744	
   745	- percentage of targeted completed analyses that crystallize successfully
   746	- percent of new analyses in the thin slice that receive a context pack
   747	- average citations per case page
   748	- contradiction rate per 100 claims
   749	- stale-claim rate
   750	- percent of runtime context tokens sourced from compiled memory vs raw evidence
   751	- delta in `insurance_risk` eval quality with and without context packs
   752	- decision-review time reduction
   753	- precedent retrieval precision on eval cases
   754	- token reduction per analysis
   755	- analyst override rate before and after compiled memory
   756	
   757	## The Deepest Fit With Orbital Inspect
   758	
   759	The deepest overlap between Karpathy's latest thinking and Orbital Inspect is this:
   760	
   761	- Karpathy: the bottleneck is not reading, it is maintaining and reusing synthesized knowledge
   762	- Orbital Inspect: the bottleneck is not collecting more orbital data, it is turning evidence into reusable operational intelligence
   763	
   764	That is why this gist matters here.
   765	
   766	Orbital Inspect already knows how to gather evidence and produce a result.
   767	The next moat is making each result permanently improve the next one.
   768	
   769	## Bottom Line
   770	
   771	Karpathy's `llm-wiki` should help Orbital Inspect in one specific way:
   772	
   773	It should push the product from "provable per-case reasoning" to "provable per-case reasoning plus compounding institutional memory."
   774	
   775	Rohit's `LLM Wiki v2` is helpful because it identifies the missing production mechanics:
   776	
   777	- lifecycle
   778	- supersession
   779	- graph structure
   780	- automation
   781	- quality control
   782	- collaboration
   783	
   784	But the implementation for this repo must be stricter than either gist:
   785	
   786	- database-first for canonical claims
   787	- provenance-first for every compiled assertion
   788	- governance-first for runtime eligibility
   789	- tenant-aware and classification-aware throughout
   790	
   791	But the first implementation should also be thinner than this memo originally proposed:
   792	
   793	- one agent before five
   794	- one compounding demo before a platform
   795	- inspectable case pages before heavy abstraction
   796	- proven uplift before graph and retrieval expansion
   797	
   798	If built that way, this is not a side feature.
   799	It is the architecture that can make Orbital Inspect meaningfully smarter every week without becoming less trustworthy.
   800

/bin/bash -lc "nl -ba brainstorming/autonomous-intelligence-layer-plan.md | sed -n '261,620p'" in /mnt/c/Users/kiran/myprojects/orbital-inspect
 succeeded in 0ms:
   261	
   262	- `backend/main.py` — mount harness router (+3 lines)
   263	- `backend/config.py` — add HARNESS_ENABLED, HARNESS_SLACK_WEBHOOK_URL, A2A_MESSAGE_TTL_SECONDS (+8 lines)

   267	- `backend/services/fleet_ingestion_service.py` — call TriggerService.evaluate_event("tle_update") after ingestion (+5 lines)
   268	- `backend/services/alert_service.py` — call TriggerService.evaluate_event(alert.alert_type) after alert generation (+5 lines)
   269	
   270	### Safety Controls
   271	
   272	| Risk | Mitigation |
   273	|------|------------|
   274	| Cost runaway | time_budget_seconds + max_iterations hard limits; cost_tracker enforcement |
   275	| Offline → runtime contamination | dataset_id column + sandbox enforcer blocks runtime evidence writes |
   276	| A2A circular loops | TTL on messages + depth counter (max 5) |
   277	| Knowledge unbounded growth | Retention decay + consolidation reduces working-tier facts |
   278	| Harness overhead | Feature-flagged; session creation is async, non-blocking |
   279	| Schema migration risk | All additive (new tables only), zero existing column changes |
   280	
   281	### Verification
   282	
   283	- [ ] Pipeline creates agent sessions when HARNESS_ENABLED=true
   284	- [ ] TLE data arrival triggers registered agent
   285	- [ ] A2A messages deliver between agents and persist
   286	- [ ] Sandbox prevents offline eval writes to runtime evidence
   287	- [ ] Multi-channel output dispatches to webhook + SSE simultaneously
   288	- [ ] Agent memory persists across sessions
   289	- [ ] HARNESS_ENABLED=false → pipeline runs identically to current behavior
   290	
   291	---
   292	
   293	## Migration Strategy
   294	
   295	3 new Alembic migrations, all purely additive:
   296	
   297	| Migration | Tables | Indexes |
   298	|-----------|--------|---------|
   299	| `0008_autoresearch_layer` | research_sessions, research_hypotheses | (org_id, status), (asset_id), (session_id, iteration) |
   300	| `0009_knowledge_crystallization` | knowledge_facts, knowledge_relationships | (org_id, fact_type), (org_id, tier), (domain), (source, target, type) |
   301	| `0010_agent_harness` | agent_instances, agent_sessions, agent_triggers, agent_messages, agent_memory | (org_id, agent_type), (agent_id, status), (to_agent_id, status) |
   302	
   303	Zero existing columns altered. Zero downtime deployment.
   304	
   305	---
   306	
   307	## Implementation Order (If Time Constrained)
   308	
   309	1. **Layer 1** (Autoresearch) — The core innovation. Without this, it's just another inspection tool.
   310	2. **Layer 2** (Knowledge) — Without this, autoresearch can't learn from history.
   311	3. **Layer 3** (Harness) — Without this, it needs human trigger. Important but additive.
   312	
   313	---

   399	
   400	async def backfill_decisions(
   401	    *,
   402	    session,
   403	    org_id: str | None = None,
   404	    limit: int = 500,
   405	) -> int:
   406	    repo = AnalysisRepository(session)
   407	    analyses = await repo.list_for_decision_backfill(org_id=org_id, limit=limit)
   408	    processed = 0
   409	    for analysis in analyses:
   410	        await post_analysis_complete(
   411	            analysis_id=analysis.id,
   412	            session=session,
   413	            actor_id="system:decision-backfill",
   414	        )
   415	        processed += 1
   416	    return processed
   417	
   418	
   419	def apply_review_action(
   420	    *,
   421	    current_status: str,
   422	    action: str,
   423	    override_action: str | None = None,
   424	    actor_is_admin: bool = False,
   425	) -> tuple[str, str | None]:
   426	    if current_status not in {"pending_human_review", "approved_for_use", "blocked"}:
   427	        raise ValueError(f"Decision review not allowed from {current_status}")
   428	
   429	    if action == "approve":
   430	        if current_status == "blocked":
   431	            raise ValueError("Blocked decisions must be reset before approval")
   432	        return "approved_for_use", None
   433	    if action == "reset_review":
   434	        return "pending_human_review", None
   435	    if action == "block":
   436	        return "blocked", None
   437	    if action == "request_reimage":
   438	        return "blocked", "reimage"
   439	    if action == "override_action":
   440	        if not actor_is_admin:
   441	            raise ValueError("Only admins may override recommended action")
   442	        if current_status == "blocked":
   443	            raise ValueError("Blocked decisions must be reset before override")
   444	        if not override_action:
   445	            raise ValueError("override_action is required")
   446	        return "approved_for_use", override_action
   447	    raise ValueError(f"Unsupported review action: {action}")

   328	# ── list_asset_evidence offline_eval leak guardrail ──────────────────
   329	
   330	
   331	@pytest.mark.asyncio
   332	async def test_list_asset_evidence_excludes_offline_eval(
   333	    session: AsyncSession, org: Organization
   334	):
   335	    """offline_eval evidence must NOT be returned by list_asset_evidence.
   336	
   337	    This is the API-layer leak: even though offline_eval records cannot be
   338	    *linked* to analyses, they were still surfaced through the asset detail
   339	    endpoint.  The fix is a .where() filter inside list_asset_evidence.
   340	    """
   341	    asset_repo = AssetRepository(session)
   342	    evidence_repo = EvidenceRepository(session)
   343	
   344	    asset = await asset_repo.resolve_or_create(
   345	        org_id=org.id, norad_id="99001", asset_type="satellite", name="TestSat",
   346	    )
   347	
   348	    # Create an offline_eval record attached to the asset.
   349	    offline_record = await evidence_repo.create_record(
   350	        org_id=org.id,
   351	        asset_id=asset.id,
   352	        source_type="benchmark_corpus",
   353	        evidence_role="offline_eval",
   354	        provider="SPEED+",
   355	        payload_json={"domain": "lightbox"},
   356	    )
   357	
   358	    results = await evidence_repo.list_asset_evidence(asset_id=asset.id)
   359	    result_ids = [r.id for r in results]
   360	
   361	    assert offline_record.id not in result_ids, (
   362	        "list_asset_evidence must not expose offline_eval evidence records"
   363	    )
   364

   401	):
   402	    """count_asset_evidence_summary must return total_count == 15 when 15
   403	    non-offline_eval records exist, even though list_asset_evidence limit=12."""
   404	    asset_repo = AssetRepository(session)
   405	    evidence_repo = EvidenceRepository(session)
   406	
   407	    asset = await asset_repo.resolve_or_create(
   408	        org_id=org.id, norad_id="88001", asset_type="satellite", name="CountSat",
   409	    )
   410	
   411	    roles = ["runtime", "public_data", "telemetry"]
   412	    for i in range(15):
   413	        await evidence_repo.create_record(
   414	            org_id=org.id,
   415	            asset_id=asset.id,
   416	            source_type="celestrak",
   417	            evidence_role=roles[i % len(roles)],
   418	            provider="CelesTrak",
   419	            payload_json={"seq": i},
   420	        )
   421	
   422	    total, counts_by_role, counts_by_source_type, providers, latest = (
   423	        await evidence_repo.count_asset_evidence_summary(asset_id=asset.id)
   424	    )
   425	
   426	    assert total == 15, f"Expected 15 total records, got {total}"
   427	    assert sum(counts_by_role.values()) == 15
   428	    assert counts_by_role.get("runtime") == 5
   429	    assert counts_by_role.get("public_data") == 5
   430	    assert counts_by_role.get("telemetry") == 5
   431	
   432	
   433	@pytest.mark.asyncio
   434	async def test_count_summary_vs_list_limit(
   435	    session: AsyncSession, org: Organization
   436	):
   437	    """list_asset_evidence(limit=12) returns only 12 records while
   438	    count_asset_evidence_summary returns the true total of 15."""
   439	    asset_repo = AssetRepository(session)
   440	    evidence_repo = EvidenceRepository(session)
   441	
   442	    asset = await asset_repo.resolve_or_create(
   443	        org_id=org.id, norad_id="88002", asset_type="satellite", name="LimitSat",
   444	    )
   445	
   446	    for i in range(15):
   447	        await evidence_repo.create_record(
   448	            org_id=org.id,
   449	            asset_id=asset.id,
   450	            source_type="celestrak",
   451	            evidence_role="runtime",
   452	            provider="CelesTrak",
   453	            payload_json={"seq": i},
   454	        )
   455	
   456	    limited = await evidence_repo.list_asset_evidence(asset_id=asset.id, limit=12)
   457	    assert len(limited) == 12, (
   458	        f"list_asset_evidence(limit=12) should return 12 records, got {len(limited)}"
   459	    )
   460	
   461	    total, _, _, _, _ = await evidence_repo.count_asset_evidence_summary(asset_id=asset.id)
   462	    assert total == 15, (
   463	        f"count_asset_evidence_summary should return 15 (full dataset), got {total}"
   464	    )

   467	@pytest.mark.asyncio
   468	async def test_count_summary_excludes_offline_eval(
   469	    session: AsyncSession, org: Organization
   470	):
   471	    """count_asset_evidence_summary must exclude offline_eval records from
   472	    total_count and all grouping dicts."""
   473	    asset_repo = AssetRepository(session)
   474	    evidence_repo = EvidenceRepository(session)
   475	
   476	    asset = await asset_repo.resolve_or_create(
   477	        org_id=org.id, norad_id="88003", asset_type="satellite", name="ExcludeSat",
   478	    )
   479	
   480	    for i in range(5):
   481	        await evidence_repo.create_record(
   482	            org_id=org.id,
   483	            asset_id=asset.id,
   484	            source_type="celestrak",
   485	            evidence_role="runtime",
   486	            provider="CelesTrak",
   487	            payload_json={"seq": i},
   488	        )
   489	
   490	    # Add one offline_eval record — must NOT be counted.
   491	    await evidence_repo.create_record(
   492	        org_id=org.id,
   493	        asset_id=asset.id,
   494	        source_type="benchmark_corpus",
   495	        evidence_role="offline_eval",
   496	        provider="SPEED+",
   497	        payload_json={"domain": "lightbox"},
   498	    )
   499	
   500	    total, counts_by_role, counts_by_source_type, providers, latest = (
   501	        await evidence_repo.count_asset_evidence_summary(asset_id=asset.id)
   502	    )
   503	
   504	    assert total == 5, (
   505	        f"Expected 5 (offline_eval excluded), got {total}"
   506	    )
   507	    assert "offline_eval" not in counts_by_role, (
   508	        "offline_eval must not appear in counts_by_role"
   509	    )
   510	    assert counts_by_source_type.get("benchmark_corpus", 0) == 0, (
   511	        "benchmark_corpus from offline_eval must not appear in counts_by_source_type"
   512	    )

   627	    async def update_metadata(
   628	        self,
   629	        asset_id: str,
   630	        *,
   631	        norad_id: str | None = None,
   632	        external_asset_id: str | None = None,
   633	        name: str | None = None,
   634	        operator_name: str | None = None,
   635	        status: str | None = None,
   636	        current_analysis_id: str | None = None,
   637	    ) -> None:
   638	        values = {}
   639	        if norad_id is not None:
   640	            values["norad_id"] = norad_id
   641	        if external_asset_id is not None:
   642	            values["external_asset_id"] = external_asset_id
   643	        if name is not None:
   644	            values["name"] = name
   645	        if operator_name is not None:
   646	            values["operator_name"] = operator_name
   647	        if status is not None:
   648	            values["status"] = status
   649	        if current_analysis_id is not None:
   650	            values["current_analysis_id"] = current_analysis_id
   651	        if not values:
   652	            return
   653	        values["updated_at"] = datetime.now(timezone.utc)
   654	        await self.session.execute(update(Asset).where(Asset.id == asset_id).values(**values))
   655	        await self.session.commit()
   656	
   657	    async def promote_current_analysis(
   658	        self,
   659	        *,
   660	        asset_id: str,
   661	        analysis: Analysis,
   662	    ) -> None:
   663	        asset = await self.get(asset_id)
   664	        if not asset:
   665	            return
   666	        if not asset.current_analysis_id:
   667	            await self.update_metadata(asset_id, current_analysis_id=analysis.id)
   668	            return
   669	        if asset.current_analysis_id == analysis.id:
   670	            return
   671	
   672	        result = await self.session.execute(
   673	            select(Analysis).where(Analysis.id == asset.current_analysis_id)
   674	        )
   675	        current = result.scalar_one_or_none()
   676	        current_ts = (
   677	            getattr(current, "completed_at", None)
   678	            or getattr(current, "created_at", None)
   679	            or datetime.min.replace(tzinfo=timezone.utc)
   680	        )
   681	        candidate_ts = (
   682	            getattr(analysis, "completed_at", None)
   683	            or getattr(analysis, "created_at", None)
   684	            or datetime.min.replace(tzinfo=timezone.utc)
   685	        )
   686	        if candidate_ts >= current_ts:
   687	            await self.update_metadata(asset_id, current_analysis_id=analysis.id)
   688	
   689	    async def resolve_or_create_subsystem(
   690	        self,
   691	        *,
   692	        asset_id: str,
   693	        org_id: str | None,
   694	        subsystem_key: str | None,
   695	        display_name: str | None = None,
   696	        subsystem_type: str | None = None,
   697	    ) -> AssetSubsystem | None:
   698	        key = (subsystem_key or "").strip().lower()
   699	        if not key:
   700	            return None
   701	        result = await self.session.execute(
   702	            select(AssetSubsystem)
   703	            .where(AssetSubsystem.asset_id == asset_id)
   704	            .where(AssetSubsystem.subsystem_key == key)
   705	            .order_by(AssetSubsystem.created_at.asc())
   706	            .limit(1)
   707	        )
   708	        subsystem = result.scalar_one_or_none()
   709	        if subsystem:
   710	            dirty = False
   711	            if display_name and not subsystem.display_name:
   712	                subsystem.display_name = display_name
   713	                dirty = True
   714	            if subsystem_type and not subsystem.subsystem_type:
   715	                subsystem.subsystem_type = subsystem_type
   716	                dirty = True
   717	            if dirty:
   718	                await self.session.commit()
   719	                await self.session.refresh(subsystem)
   720	            return subsystem
   721	
   722	        subsystem = AssetSubsystem(
   723	            asset_id=asset_id,
   724	            org_id=org_id,
   725	            subsystem_key=key,
   726	            display_name=display_name or subsystem_key,
   727	            subsystem_type=subsystem_type or key,
   728	            status="active",
   729	        )
   730	        self.session.add(subsystem)
   731	        await self.session.commit()
   732	        await self.session.refresh(subsystem)

   735	    async def count_prior_attentionworthy_analyses(
   736	        self,
   737	        *,
   738	        asset_id: str,
   739	        current_analysis_id: str,
   740	    ) -> int:
   741	        attentionworthy = (
   742	            select(func.count(Analysis.id))
   743	            .where(Analysis.asset_id == asset_id)
   744	            .where(Analysis.id != current_analysis_id)
   745	            .where(Analysis.status.in_(("completed", "completed_partial")))
   746	            .where(
   747	                (Analysis.decision_recommended_action.in_(("reimage", "maneuver_review", "servicing_candidate", "insurance_escalation", "disposal_review")))
   748	                | (Analysis.decision_status == "blocked")
   749	                | (Analysis.report_completeness == "PARTIAL")
   750	            )
   751	        )
   752	        result = await self.session.execute(attentionworthy)
   753	        return int(result.scalar() or 0)
   754	
   755	    async def _find_by_alias(
   756	        self,
   757	        *,
   758	        org_id: str | None,
   759	        asset_type: str,
   760	        alias_type: str,
   761	        alias_value: str,
   762	    ) -> Asset | None:
   763	        result = await self.session.execute(
   764	            select(Asset)
   765	            .join(AssetAlias, AssetAlias.asset_id == Asset.id)
   766	            .where(Asset.org_id == org_id)
   767	            .where(Asset.asset_type == asset_type)
   768	            .where(AssetAlias.alias_type == alias_type)
   769	            .where(AssetAlias.alias_value == alias_value)
   770	            .order_by(Asset.created_at.asc())
   771	            .limit(1)
   772	        )
   773	        return result.scalar_one_or_none()
   774	
   775	    async def _register_aliases(
   776	        self,
   777	        *,
   778	        asset: Asset,
   779	        norad_id: str | None,
   780	        external_asset_id: str | None,
   781	        display_name: str | None,
   782	        alias_candidates: dict[str, str] | None = None,
   783	    ) -> None:
   784	        if norad_id:
   785	            await self.upsert_alias(
   786	                asset_id=asset.id,
   787	                org_id=asset.org_id,
   788	                alias_type="norad",
   789	                alias_value=norad_id,
   790	                is_primary=True,
   791	            )
   792	        if external_asset_id:
   793	            await self.upsert_alias(
   794	                asset_id=asset.id,
   795	                org_id=asset.org_id,
   796	                alias_type="external_id",
   797	                alias_value=external_asset_id,
   798	                is_primary=True,
   799	            )
   800	        if display_name:
   801	            await self.upsert_alias(
   802	                asset_id=asset.id,
   803	                org_id=asset.org_id,
   804	                alias_type="display_name",
   805	                alias_value=display_name.strip(),
   806	                is_primary=bool(asset.name and asset.name.strip() == display_name.strip()),
   807	            )
   808	        for alias_type, alias_value in (alias_candidates or {}).items():
   809	            if alias_type in {"norad", "external_id", "display_name"}:
   810	                continue
   811	            await self.upsert_alias(
   812	                asset_id=asset.id,
   813	                org_id=asset.org_id,
   814	                alias_type=alias_type,
   815	                alias_value=alias_value,
   816	                is_primary=(
   817	                    alias_type == "operator_asset_id"
   818	                    and ((external_asset_id and alias_value == external_asset_id) or not external_asset_id)
   819	                ),
   820	            )
   821	
   822	    async def upsert_alias(
   823	        self,
   824	        *,
   825	        asset_id: str,
   826	        org_id: str | None,
   827	        alias_type: str,
   828	        alias_value: str,
   829	        is_primary: bool = False,
   830	    ) -> None:
   831	        value = alias_value.strip()
   832	        if not value:
   833	            return
   834	        result = await self.session.execute(
   835	            select(AssetAlias)
   836	            .where(AssetAlias.asset_id == asset_id)
   837	            .where(AssetAlias.alias_type == alias_type)
   838	            .where(AssetAlias.alias_value == value)
   839	            .limit(1)
   840	        )
   841	        existing = result.scalar_one_or_none()
   842	        if existing:
   843	            if is_primary and not existing.is_primary:
   844	                existing.is_primary = True
   845	                await self.session.commit()
   846	            return
   847	        alias = AssetAlias(
   848	            asset_id=asset_id,
   849	            org_id=org_id,
   850	            alias_type=alias_type,
   851	            alias_value=value,
   852	            is_primary=is_primary,
   853	        )
   854	        self.session.add(alias)
   855	        await self.session.commit()
   856	
   857	    async def list_fleet_assets(
   858	        self,
   859	        org_id: str | None = None,
   860	        limit: int = 500,
   861	    ) -> list:
   862	        """List all active assets with NORAD IDs for fleet ingestion."""
   863	        from db.models import Asset
   864	        stmt = select(Asset).where(Asset.norad_id.isnot(None))
   865	        if org_id is not None:
   866	            stmt = stmt.where(Asset.org_id == org_id)
   867	        stmt = stmt.order_by(Asset.updated_at.desc()).limit(limit)
   868	        result = await self.session.execute(stmt)
   869	        return list(result.scalars().all())

   922	    async def upsert_record(
   923	        self,
   924	        *,
   925	        org_id: str | None,
   926	        asset_id: str | None,
   927	        subsystem_id: str | None = None,
   928	        source_type: str,
   929	        evidence_role: str = "runtime",
   930	        provider: str | None = None,
   931	        external_ref: str | None = None,
   932	        captured_at=None,
   933	        payload_json: dict | None = None,
   934	        artifact_uri: str | None = None,
   935	        source_url: str | None = None,
   936	        license: str | None = None,
   937	        redistribution_policy: str | None = None,
   938	        confidence: float | None = None,
   939	        geometry_metadata: dict | None = None,
   940	        tags: list | None = None,
   941	    ) -> EvidenceRecord:
   942	        existing = None
   943	        if external_ref:
   944	            query = select(EvidenceRecord).where(EvidenceRecord.source_type == source_type).where(EvidenceRecord.external_ref == external_ref)
   945	            if asset_id is not None:
   946	                query = query.where(EvidenceRecord.asset_id == asset_id)
   947	            if org_id is not None:
   948	                query = query.where(EvidenceRecord.org_id == org_id)
   949	            result = await self.session.execute(query.order_by(EvidenceRecord.ingested_at.desc()).limit(1))
   950	            existing = result.scalar_one_or_none()
   951	        if existing:
   952	            existing.evidence_role = evidence_role
   953	            existing.provider = provider
   954	            existing.captured_at = captured_at or existing.captured_at
   955	            existing.payload_json = payload_json or existing.payload_json or {}
   956	            existing.artifact_uri = artifact_uri or existing.artifact_uri
   957	            existing.source_url = source_url or existing.source_url
   958	            existing.license = license or existing.license
   959	            existing.redistribution_policy = redistribution_policy or existing.redistribution_policy
   960	            existing.confidence = confidence if confidence is not None else existing.confidence
   961	            existing.geometry_metadata = geometry_metadata or existing.geometry_metadata or {}
   962	            existing.tags = tags or existing.tags or []
   963	            existing.ingested_at = datetime.now(timezone.utc)
   964	            await self.session.commit()
   965	            await self.session.refresh(existing)
   966	            return existing
   967	        return await self.create_record(
   968	            org_id=org_id,
   969	            asset_id=asset_id,
   970	            subsystem_id=subsystem_id,
   971	            source_type=source_type,
   972	            evidence_role=evidence_role,
   973	            provider=provider,
   974	            external_ref=external_ref,
   975	            captured_at=captured_at,
   976	            payload_json=payload_json,
   977	            artifact_uri=artifact_uri,
   978	            source_url=source_url,
   979	            license=license,
   980	            redistribution_policy=redistribution_policy,
   981	            confidence=confidence,
   982	            geometry_metadata=geometry_metadata,
   983	            tags=tags,
   984	        )
