   986	    async def link_analysis_evidence(
   987	        self,
   988	        *,
   989	        analysis_id: str,
   990	        evidence_id: str,
   991	        used_for: str | None = None,
   992	    ) -> AnalysisEvidenceLink:
   993	        if not await self.validate_evidence_not_offline_eval(evidence_id):
   994	            raise ValueError(
   995	                f"Evidence record {evidence_id} has role 'offline_eval' and cannot "
   996	                "be linked to a runtime analysis. Benchmark datasets must stay out "
   997	                "of customer evidence paths."
   998	            )
   999	        query = (
  1000	            select(AnalysisEvidenceLink)
  1001	            .where(AnalysisEvidenceLink.analysis_id == analysis_id)
  1002	            .where(AnalysisEvidenceLink.evidence_id == evidence_id)
  1003	            .where(AnalysisEvidenceLink.used_for == used_for)
  1004	            .limit(1)
  1005	        )
  1006	        result = await self.session.execute(query)
  1007	        existing = result.scalar_one_or_none()
  1008	        if existing:
  1009	            return existing
  1010	        link = AnalysisEvidenceLink(
  1011	            analysis_id=analysis_id,
  1012	            evidence_id=evidence_id,
  1013	            used_for=used_for,
  1014	        )
  1015	        self.session.add(link)
  1016	        await self.session.commit()
  1017	        await self.session.refresh(link)
  1018	        return link
  1019	
  1020	    async def list_analysis_evidence(
  1021	        self,
  1022	        *,
  1023	        analysis_id: str,
  1024	    ) -> list[tuple[AnalysisEvidenceLink, EvidenceRecord]]:
  1025	        result = await self.session.execute(
  1026	            select(AnalysisEvidenceLink, EvidenceRecord)
  1027	            .join(EvidenceRecord, EvidenceRecord.id == AnalysisEvidenceLink.evidence_id)
  1028	            .where(AnalysisEvidenceLink.analysis_id == analysis_id)
  1029	            .order_by(AnalysisEvidenceLink.created_at.asc())
  1030	        )
  1031	        return list(result.all())
  1032	
  1033	    async def list_asset_evidence(
  1034	        self,
  1035	        *,
  1036	        asset_id: str,
  1037	        org_id: str | None = None,
  1038	        limit: int | None = 25,
  1039	    ) -> list[EvidenceRecord]:
  1040	        query = (
  1041	            select(EvidenceRecord)
  1042	            .where(EvidenceRecord.asset_id == asset_id)
  1043	            .where(or_(EvidenceRecord.evidence_role != "offline_eval", EvidenceRecord.evidence_role.is_(None)))
  1044	            .order_by(
  1045	                EvidenceRecord.captured_at.desc().nullslast(),
  1046	                EvidenceRecord.ingested_at.desc(),
  1047	            )
  1048	        )
  1049	        if limit is not None:
  1050	            query = query.limit(limit)
  1051	        if org_id:
  1052	            query = query.where(EvidenceRecord.org_id == org_id)
  1053	        result = await self.session.execute(query)
  1054	        return list(result.scalars().all())
  1055	
  1056	    async def count_asset_evidence_summary(
  1057	        self,
  1058	        *,
  1059	        asset_id: str,
  1060	        org_id: str | None = None,
  1061	    ) -> tuple[int, dict[str, int], dict[str, int], list[str], datetime | None]:
  1062	        """Return summary aggregates for non-offline_eval asset evidence.
  1063	
  1064	        Unlike list_asset_evidence this query carries no LIMIT so the counts
  1065	        always reflect the full dataset.
  1066	        """
  1067	        base_filter = [
  1068	            EvidenceRecord.asset_id == asset_id,
  1069	            or_(EvidenceRecord.evidence_role != "offline_eval", EvidenceRecord.evidence_role.is_(None)),
  1070	        ]
  1071	        if org_id:
  1072	            base_filter.append(EvidenceRecord.org_id == org_id)
  1073	
  1074	        # total count
  1075	        total_result = await self.session.execute(
  1076	            select(func.count()).select_from(EvidenceRecord).where(*base_filter)
  1077	        )
  1078	        total_count: int = total_result.scalar_one()
  1079	
  1080	        # counts grouped by evidence_role
  1081	        role_result = await self.session.execute(
  1082	            select(EvidenceRecord.evidence_role, func.count())
  1083	            .where(*base_filter)
  1084	            .group_by(EvidenceRecord.evidence_role)
  1085	        )
  1086	        counts_by_role: dict[str, int] = {
  1087	            (row[0] or "unknown"): row[1] for row in role_result.all()
  1088	        }
  1089	
  1090	        # counts grouped by source_type
  1091	        stype_result = await self.session.execute(
  1092	            select(EvidenceRecord.source_type, func.count())
  1093	            .where(*base_filter)
  1094	            .group_by(EvidenceRecord.source_type)
  1095	        )
  1096	        counts_by_source_type: dict[str, int] = {
  1097	            (row[0] or "unknown"): row[1] for row in stype_result.all()
  1098	        }
  1099	
  1100	        # distinct providers (preserve original provider name, fall back to
  1101	        # source_type titleized for provider-less records)
  1102	        provider_result = await self.session.execute(
  1103	            select(EvidenceRecord.provider, EvidenceRecord.source_type)
  1104	            .where(*base_filter)
  1105	            .group_by(EvidenceRecord.provider, EvidenceRecord.source_type)
  1106	        )
  1107	        seen_labels: set[str] = set()
  1108	        for row in provider_result.all():
  1109	            provider_val, source_type_val = row
  1110	            if provider_val and provider_val.strip():
  1111	                seen_labels.add(provider_val.strip())
  1112	            elif source_type_val:
  1113	                seen_labels.add(source_type_val.replace("_", " ").title())
  1114	        distinct_providers: list[str] = sorted(seen_labels)
  1115	
  1116	        # latest captured_at (or ingested_at as fallback)
  1117	        latest_result = await self.session.execute(
  1118	            select(func.max(func.coalesce(EvidenceRecord.captured_at, EvidenceRecord.ingested_at)))
  1119	            .where(*base_filter)
  1120	        )
  1121	        latest_captured = latest_result.scalar()
  1122	
  1123	        return total_count, counts_by_role, counts_by_source_type, distinct_providers, latest_captured
  1124	
  1125	    async def get_asset_reference_profile(
  1126	        self,
  1127	        *,
  1128	        asset_id: str,
  1129	        org_id: str | None = None,
  1130	    ) -> AssetReferenceProfile | None:

  1135	        )
  1136	        if org_id:
  1137	            query = query.where(AssetReferenceProfile.org_id == org_id)

  1141	    async def reassign_analysis_evidence(
  1142	        self,
  1143	        *,
  1144	        analysis_id: str,
  1145	        asset_id: str,
  1146	        subsystem_id: str | None = None,
  1147	    ) -> None:
  1148	        linked = await self.list_analysis_evidence(analysis_id=analysis_id)
  1149	        dirty = False
  1150	        for _link, record in linked:
  1151	            if record.asset_id != asset_id:
  1152	                record.asset_id = asset_id
  1153	                dirty = True
  1154	            if subsystem_id is not None and record.subsystem_id != subsystem_id:
  1155	                record.subsystem_id = subsystem_id
  1156	                dirty = True
  1157	        if dirty:
  1158	            await self.session.commit()

  1212	            reference_sources_json=reference_sources_json or [],
  1213	            last_verified_at=last_verified_at,
  1214	        )
  1215	        self.session.add(profile)
  1216	        await self.session.commit()
  1217	        await self.session.refresh(profile)

  1320	    async def list_datasets(
  1321	        self,
  1322	        *,
  1323	        org_id: str | None = None,
  1324	        dataset_type: str | None = None,
  1325	        intended_use: str | None = None,
  1326	    ) -> list[DatasetRegistry]:
  1327	        query = select(DatasetRegistry).order_by(DatasetRegistry.name.asc())
  1328	        if org_id is not None:
  1329	            query = query.where(
  1330	                (DatasetRegistry.org_id == org_id) | DatasetRegistry.org_id.is_(None)
  1331	            )
  1332	        else:
  1333	            query = query.where(DatasetRegistry.org_id.is_(None))
  1334	        if dataset_type:
  1335	            query = query.where(DatasetRegistry.dataset_type == dataset_type)
  1336	        if intended_use:
  1337	            query = query.where(DatasetRegistry.intended_use == intended_use)
  1338	        result = await self.session.execute(query)
  1339	        return list(result.scalars().all())
  1340	
  1341	    async def get_dataset(
  1342	        self,
  1343	        dataset_id: str,
  1344	        *,
  1345	        org_id: str | None = None,
  1346	    ) -> DatasetRegistry | None:
  1347	        query = select(DatasetRegistry).where(DatasetRegistry.id == dataset_id)
  1348	        if org_id is not None:
  1349	            query = query.where(
  1350	                (DatasetRegistry.org_id == org_id) | DatasetRegistry.org_id.is_(None)
  1351	            )
  1352	        result = await self.session.execute(query)
  1353	        return result.scalar_one_or_none()
  1354	
  1355	    async def validate_evidence_not_offline_eval(
  1356	        self,
  1357	        evidence_id: str,
  1358	    ) -> bool:
  1359	        """Return True if the evidence record is safe to link to a runtime analysis.
  1360	
  1361	        Returns False when the record carries evidence_role='offline_eval',
  1362	        which must never leak into customer-facing analysis paths.
  1363	        """
  1364	        result = await self.session.execute(
  1365	            select(EvidenceRecord.evidence_role)
  1366	            .where(EvidenceRecord.id == evidence_id)
  1367	            .limit(1)
  1368	        )
  1369	        role = result.scalar_one_or_none()
  1370	        return role != "offline_eval"
  1371	
  1372	
  1373	class ReportRepository:
  1374	    """CRUD operations for condition reports."""
  1375	
  1376	    def __init__(self, session: AsyncSession):
  1377	        self.session = session
  1378	
  1379	    async def create(
  1380	        self,
  1381	        analysis_id: str,
  1382	        full_report: dict,
  1383	        *,
  1384	        governance_summary: dict | None = None,
  1385	        human_review_required: bool = True,
  1386	    ) -> Report:
  1387	        """Create a draft report from analysis results."""
  1388	        report = Report(
  1389	            analysis_id=analysis_id,
  1390	            full_report_json=full_report,
  1391	            status="DRAFT",
  1392	            governance_summary=governance_summary or {},
  1393	            human_review_required=human_review_required,
  1394	        )
  1395	        self.session.add(report)
  1396	        await self.session.commit()
  1397	        await self.session.refresh(report)
  1398	        return report
  1399	
  1400	    async def get(self, report_id: str, org_id: str | None = None) -> Report | None:
  1401	        query = select(Report).where(Report.id == report_id)
  1402	        if org_id:
  1403	            query = query.join(Analysis).where(Analysis.org_id == org_id)
  1404	        result = await self.session.execute(query)
  1405	        return result.scalar_one_or_none()

   746	        baseline_reference=_safe_json_form(baseline_reference, "baseline_reference"),
   747	        user=user,
   748	        request_id=getattr(request.state, "request_id", None),
   749	    )

   762	        "status": "dispatched" if dispatch["dispatch_mode"] == "arq" else "queued",

   772	@app.post("/api/v1/analyze")
   773	async def analyze(
   774	    image: UploadFile = File(...),
   775	    norad_id: str = Form(default=""),
   776	    context: str = Form(default=""),
   777	    asset_type: str = Form(default="satellite"),
   778	    asset_name: str = Form(default=""),
   779	    external_asset_id: str = Form(default=""),
   780	    inspection_epoch: str = Form(default=""),
   781	    target_subsystem: str = Form(default=""),
   782	    capture_metadata: str = Form(default=""),
   783	    telemetry_summary: str = Form(default=""),
   784	    baseline_reference: str = Form(default=""),
   785	    user: CurrentUser | None = Depends(require_role("analyst")),
   786	):
   787	    """
   788	    Legacy wrapper: preserve inline SSE behavior for one transition window.
   789	    """
   790	    if not settings.DEMO_MODE:
   791	        raise HTTPException(
   792	            status_code=410,
   793	            detail="Legacy /api/analyze is retired for production use. Submit work via POST /api/analyses instead.",
   794	            headers=_legacy_analyze_headers(),
   795	        )
   796	
   797	    uploads = await _collect_uploads(image, None)
   798	    _safe_json_form(capture_metadata, "capture_metadata")
   799	    _safe_json_form(telemetry_summary, "telemetry_summary")
   800	    _safe_json_form(baseline_reference, "baseline_reference")
   801	    _normalize_asset_type(asset_type)
   802	    asset_name.strip()
   803	    external_asset_id.strip()
   804	    inspection_epoch.strip()
   805	    target_subsystem.strip()
   806	
   807	    norad = norad_id.strip() or None
   808	    if norad and not re.fullmatch(r"\d{1,9}", norad):
   809	        raise HTTPException(status_code=400, detail="norad_id must be 1-9 digits")
   810	
   811	    _upload, image_bytes, content_type = uploads[0]
   812	
   813	    async def event_generator():
   814	        async for event in run_satellite_pipeline(
   815	            image_bytes=image_bytes,
   816	            image_mime=content_type,
   817	            norad_id=norad,
   818	            additional_context=context,
   819	        ):
   820	            yield event
   821	
   822	    return EventSourceResponse(event_generator(), headers=_legacy_analyze_headers())

   260	def _prom_escape(value: object) -> str:
   261	    return str(value).replace("\\", "\\\\").replace('"', '\\"').replace("\n", "\\n")
   262	
   263	
   264	def _prom_labels(**labels: object) -> str:
   265	    return ",".join(f'{key}="{_prom_escape(value)}"' for key, value in labels.items() if value is not None)

   269	    *,
   270	    uploads: list[tuple[UploadFile, bytes, str]],

   298	        "external_asset_id": external_asset_id or capture_metadata.get("external_asset_id") or "",
   299	    }

   303	        "external_asset_id": external_asset_id or baseline_reference.get("external_asset_id") or "",
   304	    }
   305	    stored_object = storage.store_bytes(
   306	        category="uploads",
   307	        filename=primary_upload.filename or "image.jpg",
   308	        data=primary_bytes,
   309	        content_type=primary_mime,
   310	        metadata={
   311	            "norad_id": norad or "",
   312	            "asset_type": asset_type,
   313	            "asset_name": asset_name,
   314	            "external_asset_id": external_asset_id,
   315	            "request_id": request_id or "",
   316	        },
   317	    )
   318

   323	            "satellite_name": "Deterministic E2E Asset",
   324	            "total_items": 1,

   332	        }

    14	class OrbitalRegime(str, Enum):
    15	    LEO = "LEO"       # Low Earth Orbit (200-2000km)
    16	    MEO = "MEO"       # Medium Earth Orbit (2000-35786km)
    17	    GEO = "GEO"       # Geostationary (35786km)
    18	    HEO = "HEO"       # Highly Elliptical Orbit
    19	    SSO = "SSO"       # Sun-Synchronous Orbit
    20	    UNKNOWN = "UNKNOWN"

    23	class SatelliteType(str, Enum):

    25	    EARTH_OBSERVATION = "earth_observation"
    26	    NAVIGATION = "navigation"
    27	    SCIENTIFIC = "scientific"
    28	    WEATHER = "weather"
    29	    MILITARY = "military"
    30	    TECHNOLOGY_DEMO = "technology_demo"
    31	    MEGA_CONSTELLATION = "mega_constellation"

    58	class ClassificationResult(BaseModel):
    59	    """Output of the Orbital Classification Agent."""
    60	    valid: bool = True
    61	    rejection_reason: str | None = None
    62	    satellite_type: str = "other"
    63	    bus_platform: str | None = None
    64	    orbital_regime: str = "UNKNOWN"
    65	    expected_components: list[str] = []
    66	    design_life_years: float | None = None
    67	    estimated_age_years: float | None = None
    68	    operator: str | None = None
    69	    notes: str = ""
    70	    degraded: bool = False
    71	
    72	    @field_validator("expected_components", mode="before")
    73	    @classmethod
    74	    def _normalize_expected_components(cls, value):
    75	        if value is None:
    76	            return []
    77	        if isinstance(value, str):
    78	            return [
    79	                item.strip(" -\t")
    80	                for item in value.replace("\n", ",").split(",")
    81	                if item.strip()
    82	            ]
    83	        return value
    84	
    85	
    86	class SatelliteDamageItem(BaseModel):
    87	    """Individual damage finding on a satellite."""
    88	    id: int
    89	    type: str                           # micrometeorite_crater, cell_degradation, thermal_blanket_damage, etc.
    90	    description: str
    91	    bounding_box: list[int]             # [y_min, x_min, y_max, x_max] normalized 0-1000
    92	    label: str                          # Short label for overlay (max 5 words)
    93	    severity: str                       # MINOR | MODERATE | SEVERE | CRITICAL
    94	    confidence: float                   # 0.0-1.0
    95	    uncertain: bool = False
    96	    estimated_power_impact_pct: float = 0.0  # Estimated power loss from this damage
    97	
    98	
    99	class SatelliteDamagesAssessment(BaseModel):
   100	    """Output of the Satellite Vision Agent."""
   101	    damages: list[SatelliteDamageItem] = []
   102	    overall_pattern: str = ""           # e.g., "cumulative micrometeorite bombardment"
   103	    overall_severity: str = "MINOR"
   104	    overall_confidence: float = 0.0
   105	    total_power_impact_pct: float = 0.0
   106	    healthy_areas_noted: str = ""
   107	    component_assessed: str = ""        # Which component was analyzed (solar_array, antenna, bus)
   108	    degraded: bool = False
   109	
   110	
   111	class OrbitalStressor(BaseModel):
   112	    """Environmental stressor in the orbital environment."""
   113	    name: str
   114	    severity: str                       # LOW | MEDIUM | HIGH
   115	    measured_value: str = ""
   116	    description: str = ""
   117	    source: str = ""
   118	
   119	
   120	class OrbitalEnvironmentAnalysis(BaseModel):
   121	    """Output of the Orbital Environment Agent."""
   122	    orbital_regime: str = ""
   123	    altitude_km: float | None = None
   124	    inclination_deg: float | None = None
   125	    debris_flux_density: str = ""       # particles/m²/year at this altitude
   126	    collision_probability: str = ""     # per year
   127	    radiation_dose_rate: str = ""       # rad/year
   128	    thermal_cycling_range: str = ""     # e.g., "-150°C to +150°C"
   129	    atomic_oxygen_flux: str = ""        # atoms/cm²/s
   130	    stressors: list[OrbitalStressor] = []
   131	    accelerating_factors: list[str] = []
   132	    mitigating_factors: list[str] = []
   133	    data_sources: list[str] = []
   134	    degraded: bool = False
   135	
   136	
   137	class SatellitePrecedent(BaseModel):
   138	    """Historical satellite failure/damage precedent."""
   139	    event: str
   140	    satellite: str = ""
   141	    operator: str = ""
   142	    year: str = ""
   143	    outcome: str = ""
   144	    claim_amount_usd: str = ""
   145	    relevance: str = ""
   146	    source: str = ""
   147	
   148	
   149	class SatelliteFailureModeAnalysis(BaseModel):
   150	    """Output of the Satellite Failure Mode Agent."""
   151	    failure_mode: str = ""
   152	    mechanism: str = ""
   153	    root_cause_chain: list[str] = []
   154	    progression_rate: str = "MODERATE"
   155	    power_degradation_estimate_pct: float = 0.0
   156	    remaining_life_revision_years: float | None = None
   157	    time_to_critical: str = ""
   158	    historical_precedents: list[SatellitePrecedent] = []
   159	    degraded: bool = False
   160	    probability_components: list[ProbabilityComponent] = []
   161	
   162	
   163	class RiskMatrixDimension(BaseModel):
   164	    score: int                          # 1-5
   165	    reasoning: str = ""
   166	
   167	
   168	class RiskMatrix(BaseModel):
   169	    severity: RiskMatrixDimension
   170	    probability: RiskMatrixDimension
   171	    consequence: RiskMatrixDimension
   172	    composite: int                      # 1-125
   173	
   174	
   175	class ConsistencyCheck(BaseModel):
   176	    passed: bool = True
   177	    anomalies: list[str] = []
   178	    confidence_adjustment: str = ""
   179	
   180	
   181	class UnderwritingRecommendation(str, Enum):
   182	    INSURABLE_STANDARD = "INSURABLE_STANDARD"
   183	    INSURABLE_ELEVATED_PREMIUM = "INSURABLE_ELEVATED_PREMIUM"
   184	    INSURABLE_WITH_EXCLUSIONS = "INSURABLE_WITH_EXCLUSIONS"
   185	    FURTHER_INVESTIGATION = "FURTHER_INVESTIGATION"
   186	    UNINSURABLE = "UNINSURABLE"
   187	
   188	
   189	class InsuranceRiskReport(BaseModel):
   190	    """Output of the Insurance Risk Agent — the key differentiator."""
   191	    consistency_check: ConsistencyCheck
   192	    risk_matrix: RiskMatrix
   193	    risk_tier: str                      # LOW | MEDIUM | MEDIUM-HIGH | HIGH | CRITICAL
   194	
   195	    # Insurance-specific metrics
   196	    estimated_remaining_life_years: float | None = None
   197	    power_margin_percentage: float | None = None
   198	    annual_degradation_rate_pct: float | None = None
   199	    replacement_cost_usd: float | None = None
   200	    depreciated_value_usd: float | None = None
   201	    revenue_at_risk_annual_usd: float | None = None
   202	    total_loss_probability: float | None = None  # 0.0-1.0 over remaining life
   203	
   204	    underwriting_recommendation: str = "FURTHER_INVESTIGATION"
   205	    recommendation_rationale: str = ""
   206	    recommended_actions: list[dict] = []
   207	    worst_case_scenario: str = ""
   208	    summary: str = ""
   209	    degraded: bool = False
   210	    evidence_gaps: list[str] = []
   211	    report_completeness: str = "COMPLETE"
   212	
   213	    # Deutsch Layer: Provenance & Calibration (all Optional, backward compatible)
   214	    confidence_calibration: ConfidenceCalibration | None = None
   215	    replacement_cost_detail: FinancialEstimate | None = None
   216	    depreciated_value_detail: FinancialEstimate | None = None
   217	    revenue_at_risk_detail: FinancialEstimate | None = None
   218	    loss_probability_derivation: LossProbabilityDerivation | None = None
   219	    sensitivity_analysis: SensitivityAnalysis | None = None
   220	    remaining_life_provenance: FieldProvenance | None = None
   221	    power_margin_provenance: FieldProvenance | None = None
   222	    degradation_rate_provenance: FieldProvenance | None = None
   223	
   224	
   225	class SatelliteConditionReport(BaseModel):
   226	    """Full Satellite Condition Report — the product deliverable."""
   227	    target: SatelliteTarget
   228	    classification: ClassificationResult
   229	    vision: SatelliteDamagesAssessment | None = None
   230	    environment: OrbitalEnvironmentAnalysis | None = None
   231	    failure_mode: SatelliteFailureModeAnalysis | None = None
   232	    insurance_risk: InsuranceRiskReport | None = None
   233	    generated_at: datetime = Field(default_factory=lambda: datetime.now(timezone.utc))
   234	    report_version: str = "1.0"

     1	from datetime import datetime, timedelta, timezone
     2	from types import SimpleNamespace
     3	
     4	import pytest
     5	
     6	from services.decision_policy_service import compute_triage, evaluate_decision_policy
     7	from services.post_analysis_service import apply_review_action
     8	
     9	
    10	def _analysis(
    11	    *,
    12	    status="completed",
    13	    composite=16,
    14	    risk_tier="LOW",
    15	    underwriting="INSURABLE_STANDARD",
    16	    evidence_pct=100.0,
    17	    degraded=False,
    18	    report_completeness="COMPLETE",
    19	    asset_type="satellite",
    20	    failure_reasons=None,
    21	    evidence_gaps=None,
    22	):
    23	    return SimpleNamespace(
    24	        id="analysis-1",
    25	        status=status,
    26	        asset_type=asset_type,
    27	        insurance_risk_result={
    28	            "risk_matrix": {"composite": composite},
    29	            "risk_tier": risk_tier,
    30	            "underwriting_recommendation": underwriting,
    31	            "evidence_gaps": evidence_gaps or [],
    32	        } if status not in {"failed", "rejected"} else {},
    33	        environment_result={},
    34	        evidence_completeness_pct=evidence_pct,
    35	        degraded=degraded,
    36	        failure_reasons=failure_reasons or [],
    37	        evidence_gaps=evidence_gaps or [],
    38	        human_review_required=True,
    39	        report_completeness=report_completeness,
    40	        created_at=datetime.now(timezone.utc) - timedelta(days=5),
    41	        completed_at=datetime.now(timezone.utc) - timedelta(days=2),
    42	    )
    43	
    44	
    45	def test_low_risk_sufficient_evidence_maps_to_continue_operations():
    46	    decision = evaluate_decision_policy(_analysis())
    47	    assert decision.status == "pending_human_review"
    48	    assert decision.summary["recommended_action"] == "continue_operations"
    49	    assert decision.summary["decision_confidence"] == "high"
    50	    assert decision.summary["blocked"] is False
    51	
    52	
    53	def test_partial_or_degraded_evidence_forces_reimage_or_monitor():
    54	    decision = evaluate_decision_policy(
    55	        _analysis(
    56	            composite=75,
    57	            risk_tier="HIGH",
    58	            underwriting="INSURABLE_WITH_EXCLUSIONS",
    59	            evidence_pct=45.0,
    60	            degraded=True,
    61	            report_completeness="PARTIAL",
    62	            evidence_gaps=["satellite_vision"],
    63	        )
    64	    )
    65	    assert decision.status == "pending_human_review"
    66	    assert decision.summary["recommended_action"] == "reimage"
    67	    assert decision.summary["decision_confidence"] == "low"
    68	
    69	
    70	def test_failed_analysis_is_blocked():
    71	    decision = evaluate_decision_policy(_analysis(status="failed"))
    72	    assert decision.status == "blocked"
    73	    assert decision.summary["recommended_action"] is None
    74	    assert decision.summary["blocked"] is True
    75	
    76	
    77	def test_triage_formula_respects_recurrence_and_pending_review():
    78	    analysis = _analysis(composite=80, risk_tier="HIGH", underwriting="INSURABLE_WITH_EXCLUSIONS")
    79	    decision = evaluate_decision_policy(analysis)
    80	    score, band, factors = compute_triage(
    81	        analysis,
    82	        decision_summary=decision.summary,
    83	        decision_status=decision.status,
    84	        recurrence_count=3,
    85	    )
    86	    assert score > 0.5
    87	    assert band in {"elevated", "priority", "urgent"}
    88	    assert factors["recurrence_count"] == 3
    89	
    90	
    91	def test_triage_accepts_naive_persisted_timestamps():
    92	    analysis = _analysis()
    93	    analysis.completed_at = datetime.now() - timedelta(days=1)
    94	    analysis.created_at = datetime.now() - timedelta(days=3)
    95	    decision = evaluate_decision_policy(analysis)
    96	
    97	    score, band, factors = compute_triage(
    98	        analysis,
    99	        decision_summary=decision.summary,
   100	        decision_status=decision.status,
   101	        recurrence_count=0,
   102	    )
   103	
   104	    assert score >= 0.0
   105	    assert band in {"routine", "elevated", "priority", "urgent"}
   106	    assert factors["age_days"] >= 0.0
   107

   111	        apply_review_action(current_status="blocked", action="approve")
   112

   114	def test_review_state_machine_allows_admin_override():

   116	        current_status="pending_human_review",
   117	        action="override_action",
   118	        override_action="monitor",
   119	        actor_is_admin=True,
   120	    )

   122	    assert override_action == "monitor"
   123

   125	def test_review_state_machine_rejects_override_from_blocked():

   128	            current_status="blocked",
   129	            action="override_action",

   131	            actor_is_admin=True,
   132	        )
   133	
   134

   137	        current_status="blocked",
   138	        action="reset_review",
   139	    )
   140	    assert status == "pending_human_review"
   141	    assert override_action is None

    54	def _auth_headers(role: str, org_id: str = "org-secure", extra_claims: dict | None = None) -> dict[str, str]:
    55	    token = create_access_token(
    56	        user_id=f"{role}-user",
    57	        org_id=org_id,
    58	        role=role,
    59	        extra_claims=extra_claims,
    60	    )
    61	    return {"Authorization": f"Bearer {token}"}

    67	    @model_validator(mode="after")
    68	    def validate_jwt_secret(self):
    69	        if self.AUTH_ENABLED is None:
    70	            self.AUTH_ENABLED = not self.DEMO_MODE
    71	        if self.E2E_TEST_MODE:
    72	            self.DATABASE_AUTO_INIT = True
    73	        if self.APP_ENV in {"staging", "production"} and self.DEMO_MODE:
    74	            raise ValueError("DEMO_MODE must be false in staging and production environments")
    75	        if self.APP_ENV in {"staging", "production"} and not self.AUTH_ENABLED:
    76	            raise ValueError("AUTH_ENABLED must be true in staging and production environments")
    77	        if self.APP_ENV in {"staging", "production"} and not self.WEBHOOK_SECRET_ENCRYPTION_KEY:
    78	            raise ValueError("WEBHOOK_SECRET_ENCRYPTION_KEY must be set in staging and production environments")

    80	            raise ValueError(

    82	                "Generate one with: python -c 'import secrets; print(secrets.token_urlsafe(64))'"
    83	            )

    89	            raise ValueError("APP_ENV must be one of: development, staging, production, test")
    90	        return self

   162	        configured = [
   163	            key
   164	            for key in [self.WEBHOOK_SECRET_ENCRYPTION_KEY, *self.WEBHOOK_SECRET_PREVIOUS_KEYS]
   165	            if key

   169	        digest = hashlib.sha256(f"orbital-inspect-webhooks:{self.JWT_SECRET}".encode("utf-8")).digest()

   105	
   106	class SecurityHeadersMiddleware(BaseHTTPMiddleware):
   107	    async def dispatch(self, request: Request, call_next) -> Response:
   108	        response = await call_next(request)
   109	        response.headers["X-Content-Type-Options"] = "nosniff"
   110	        response.headers["X-Frame-Options"] = "DENY"
   111	        response.headers["X-XSS-Protection"] = "1; mode=block"
   112	        response.headers["Referrer-Policy"] = "strict-origin-when-cross-origin"
   113	        response.headers["Permissions-Policy"] = "camera=(), microphone=(), geolocation=()"
   114	        if not settings.DEMO_MODE:
   115	            response.headers["Strict-Transport-Security"] = "max-age=31536000; includeSubDomains"
   116	        return response
   117	
   118	
   119	app.add_middleware(SecurityHeadersMiddleware)
   120	
   121	# ── Backward-compat redirect: /api/<path> → /api/v1/<path> ─────────
   122	# Infrastructure endpoints (health, ready, metrics) are excluded.
   123	_UNVERSIONED_PREFIXES = ("/api/health", "/api/ready", "/api/metrics")
   124	
   125	
   126	class ApiVersionRedirectMiddleware(BaseHTTPMiddleware):
   127	    """Transparently rewrite legacy /api/X requests to /api/v1/X."""
   128	
   129	    async def dispatch(self, request: Request, call_next) -> Response:
   130	        path = request.scope["path"]
   131	        if (
   132	            path.startswith("/api/")
   133	            and not path.startswith("/api/v1/")
   134	            and not any(path.startswith(p) for p in _UNVERSIONED_PREFIXES)
   135	        ):
   136	            # Rewrite path in-place (internal redirect, no 301/302)
   137	            new_path = "/api/v1/" + path[len("/api/"):]
   138	            request.scope["path"] = new_path
   139	        return await call_next(request)
   140	
   141	
   142	app.add_middleware(ApiVersionRedirectMiddleware)
   143	
   144	# Register RFC 7807 error envelope
   145	try:
   146	    from api.error_envelope import register_error_handlers
   147	    register_error_handlers(app)
   148	except ImportError:
   149	    pass
   150	
   151	# Request logging middleware
   152	try:
   153	    from middleware.request_logging import RequestLoggingMiddleware
   154	    app.add_middleware(RequestLoggingMiddleware)
   155	except ImportError:
   156	    pass
   157	
   158	# Mount versioned API router (all business endpoints under /api/v1/)

   160	    from api.v1 import mount_v1_routers
   161	    v1_router = mount_v1_routers()
   162	    app.include_router(v1_router)
   163	except ImportError:
   164	    pass

     1	"""Persistence helpers for analysis evidence bundles."""
     2	
     3	from __future__ import annotations
     4	
     5	from datetime import datetime
     6	
     7	from db.repository import EvidenceRepository
     8	from models.evidence import EvidenceBundle, EvidenceItem, EvidenceSource
     9	
    10	
    11	def _classify_item(item: EvidenceItem) -> tuple[str, str, str]:
    12	    mapping = {
    13	        EvidenceSource.IMAGERY: ("imagery", "runtime", "imagery"),
    14	        EvidenceSource.TELEMETRY: ("operator_telemetry", "runtime", "telemetry"),
    15	        EvidenceSource.TLE_HISTORY: ("celestrak", "runtime", "orbital_context"),
    16	        EvidenceSource.CONJUNCTION_RISK: ("celestrak", "runtime", "conjunction_risk"),
    17	        EvidenceSource.OPERATOR_NOTES: ("operator_notes", "runtime", "operator_notes"),
    18	        EvidenceSource.MAINTENANCE_RECORDS: ("maintenance_records", "reference", "maintenance"),
    19	        EvidenceSource.PRIOR_ANALYSIS: ("internal_prior_analysis", "runtime", "policy_context"),
    20	        EvidenceSource.SPACE_WEATHER: ("noaa_swpc", "runtime", "environment"),
    21	        EvidenceSource.DEBRIS_ENVIRONMENT: ("ordem", "runtime", "environment"),
    22	        EvidenceSource.REFERENCE_PROFILE: ("reference_profile", "reference", "baseline"),
    23	        EvidenceSource.RF_ACTIVITY: ("satnogs", "runtime", "rf_activity"),
    24	    }
    25	    return mapping[item.source]
    26	
    27	
    28	def _coerce_timestamp(value):
    29	    if not value:
    30	        return None
    31	    if isinstance(value, datetime):
    32	        return value
    33	    if isinstance(value, str):
    34	        normalized = value.replace("Z", "+00:00")
    35	        try:
    36	            return datetime.fromisoformat(normalized)
    37	        except ValueError:
    38	            return None
    39	    return None
    40	
    41	
    42	def _external_ref_for_item(item: EvidenceItem, asset_id: str | None) -> str | None:
    43	    metadata = item.metadata or {}
    44	    explicit = metadata.get("external_ref")
    45	    if explicit:
    46	        return str(explicit)
    47	    timestamp = item.timestamp or "unknown"
    48	    if item.source == EvidenceSource.IMAGERY:
    49	        return None
    50	    return f"{item.source.value}:{asset_id or 'asset'}:{timestamp}"
    51	
    52	
    53	async def persist_evidence_bundle(
    54	    session,
    55	    *,
    56	    analysis_id: str,
    57	    org_id: str | None,
    58	    asset_id: str | None,
    59	    subsystem_id: str | None,
    60	    bundle: EvidenceBundle,
    61	) -> int:
    62	    repo = EvidenceRepository(session)
    63	    linked = 0
    64	    for item in bundle.items:
    65	        source_type, evidence_role, used_for = _classify_item(item)
    66	        metadata = item.metadata or {}
    67	        record = await repo.upsert_record(
    68	            org_id=org_id,
    69	            asset_id=asset_id,
    70	            subsystem_id=subsystem_id,
    71	            source_type=source_type,
    72	            evidence_role=evidence_role,
    73	            provider=metadata.get("provider"),
    74	            external_ref=_external_ref_for_item(item, asset_id),
    75	            captured_at=_coerce_timestamp(item.timestamp),
    76	            payload_json=item.payload or {},
    77	            artifact_uri=metadata.get("storage_uri") or metadata.get("artifact_uri"),
    78	            source_url=metadata.get("source_url"),
    79	            license=metadata.get("license"),
    80	            redistribution_policy=metadata.get("redistribution_policy"),
    81	            confidence=item.confidence,
    82	            geometry_metadata=metadata.get("geometry_metadata") or {},
    83	            tags=metadata.get("tags") or [item.source.value],
    84	        )
    85	        await repo.link_analysis_evidence(
    86	            analysis_id=analysis_id,
    87	            evidence_id=record.id,
    88	            used_for=used_for,
    89	        )
    90	        linked += 1
    91	    return linked

    10

    12	def build_model_manifest() -> dict:

    21	def apply_decision_governance(
    22	    insurance_result: dict | None,

    24	    evidence_completeness_pct: float | None,
    25	    degraded: bool,
    26	    failure_reasons: list[str],
    27	) -> tuple[dict, dict]:
    28	    result = deepcopy(insurance_result or {})
    29	    blocked_reasons: list[str] = []
    30	
    31	    if evidence_completeness_pct is None:
    32	        blocked_reasons.append("evidence completeness unavailable")
    33	    elif evidence_completeness_pct < settings.MIN_EVIDENCE_COMPLETENESS_FOR_DECISION:
    34	        blocked_reasons.append(
    35	            f"evidence completeness {evidence_completeness_pct:.1f}% below policy threshold"
    36	        )
    37	
    38	    if degraded:
    39	        blocked_reasons.append("one or more pipeline stages degraded")
    40	    if failure_reasons:
    41	        blocked_reasons.append("pipeline recorded failure reasons")
    42	
    43	    if blocked_reasons:
    44	        result["underwriting_recommendation"] = "FURTHER_INVESTIGATION"
    45	        rationale = result.get("recommendation_rationale") or result.get("summary") or ""
    46	        governance_note = "Governance hold: " + "; ".join(blocked_reasons)
    47	        result["recommendation_rationale"] = (
    48	            f"{rationale} {governance_note}".strip()
    49	        )
    50	        result["summary"] = (
    51	            f"{result.get('summary', '')} {governance_note}".strip()
    52	        )
    53	        result["report_completeness"] = "PARTIAL"
    54	
    55	    governance = {
    56	        "policy_version": settings.GOVERNANCE_POLICY_VERSION,
    57	        "human_review_required": settings.REQUIRE_HUMAN_REVIEW_FOR_DECISIONS,
    58	        "decision_blocked_reason": "; ".join(blocked_reasons) if blocked_reasons else None,
    59	        "minimum_evidence_completeness_pct": settings.MIN_EVIDENCE_COMPLETENESS_FOR_DECISION,
    60	    }
    61	    return result, governance

/bin/bash -lc "nl -ba backend/models/evidence.py | sed -n '1,260p'" in /mnt/c/Users/kiran/myprojects/orbital-inspect
 succeeded in 0ms:
     1	"""
     2	Evidence fusion models for multi-source satellite intelligence.
     3	
     4	Evidence sources include imagery, telemetry, orbital history,
     5	public reference profiles, RF observations, operator maintenance
     6	records, and prior analysis results.
     7	"""
     8	
     9	from datetime import datetime, timezone
    10	from enum import Enum
    11	
    12	from pydantic import BaseModel, Field
    13	
    14	
    15	class EvidenceSource(str, Enum):
    16	    """Types of evidence that can be fused into an analysis."""
    17	
    18	    IMAGERY = "imagery"
    19	    TELEMETRY = "telemetry"
    20	    TLE_HISTORY = "tle_history"
    21	    CONJUNCTION_RISK = "conjunction_risk"
    22	    OPERATOR_NOTES = "operator_notes"
    23	    MAINTENANCE_RECORDS = "maintenance_records"
    24	    PRIOR_ANALYSIS = "prior_analysis"
    25	    SPACE_WEATHER = "space_weather"
    26	    DEBRIS_ENVIRONMENT = "debris_environment"
    27	    REFERENCE_PROFILE = "reference_profile"
    28	    RF_ACTIVITY = "rf_activity"
    29	
    30	
    31	class EvidenceItem(BaseModel):
    32	    """A single piece of evidence from any source."""
    33	
    34	    id: str = ""
    35	    source: EvidenceSource
    36	    data_type: str = ""
    37	    timestamp: str = ""
    38	    description: str = ""
    39	    confidence: float = 1.0
    40	    payload: dict = {}
    41	    metadata: dict = {}
    42	
    43	
    44	class EvidenceBundle(BaseModel):
    45	    """
    46	    Unified evidence package for a satellite.
    47	
    48	    Combines all available evidence sources into a single bundle
    49	    that agents can consume for richer, more accurate analysis.
    50	    """
    51	
    52	    satellite_id: str = ""
    53	    satellite_name: str = ""
    54	    items: list[EvidenceItem] = []
    55	
    56	    total_items: int = 0
    57	    sources_available: list[str] = []
    58	    earliest_evidence: str = ""
    59	    latest_evidence: str = ""
    60	
    61	    prior_analyses_count: int = 0
    62	    prior_risk_tiers: list[str] = []
    63	
    64	    fused_at: str = Field(default_factory=lambda: datetime.now(timezone.utc).isoformat())
    65	    fusion_confidence: float = 1.0
    66	
    67	    def add_item(self, item: EvidenceItem):
    68	        self.items.append(item)
    69	        self.total_items = len(self.items)
    70	        if item.source.value not in self.sources_available:
    71	            self.sources_available.append(item.source.value)
    72	
    73	    def to_agent_context(self) -> str:
    74	        """Convert bundle to text context for agent prompts."""
    75	        parts = [f"Evidence Bundle for {self.satellite_name or self.satellite_id}:"]
    76	        parts.append(f"  Sources: {', '.join(self.sources_available)}")
    77	        parts.append(f"  Total evidence items: {self.total_items}")
    78	
    79	        if self.prior_analyses_count > 0:
    80	            parts.append(f"  Prior analyses: {self.prior_analyses_count}")
    81	            parts.append(f"  Historical risk tiers: {' → '.join(self.prior_risk_tiers)}")
    82	
    83	        for item in self.items:
    84	            parts.append(f"\n  [{item.source.value}] {item.description}")
    85	            if item.payload:
    86	                for key, value in item.payload.items():
    87	                    if isinstance(value, str) and len(value) > 200:
    88	                        parts.append(f"    {key}: {value[:200]}...")
    89	                    else:
    90	                        parts.append(f"    {key}: {value}")
    91	
    92	        return "\n".join(parts)

    18	from models.satellite import ClassificationResult

    22

    24	def _build_agent():
    25	    if not is_adk_available():
    26	        return None
    27	
    28	    from google.adk.agents import Agent
    29	
    30	    return Agent(
    31	        name="orbital_classification_agent",
    32	        model=get_model_name(),

    35	    )

    37	
    38	_agent = None
    39	
    40	
    41	def _get_agent():
    42	    global _agent
    43	    if _agent is None:
    44	        _agent = _build_agent()
    45	    return _agent
    46	
    47	
    48	async def classify_satellite(
    49	    image_bytes: bytes,
    50	    image_mime: str = "image/jpeg",
    51	    norad_id: str | None = None,
    52	    additional_context: str = "",
    53	) -> ClassificationResult:
    54	    """
    55	    Classify a satellite from its image, optionally enriched with CelesTrak data.
    56	
    57	    Args:
    58	        image_bytes: Satellite image data
    59	        image_mime: Image MIME type
    60	        norad_id: Optional NORAD catalog number for orbital data enrichment
    61	        additional_context: Optional user-provided context
    62	
    63	    Returns:
    64	        ClassificationResult with satellite type, regime, components, design life
    65	    """
    66	    # Enrich with CelesTrak data if NORAD ID provided
    67	    celestrak_context = ""
    68	    if norad_id:
    69	        try:
    70	            from services.celestrak_service import lookup_by_norad_id
    71	            sat_data = await lookup_by_norad_id(norad_id)
    72	            if sat_data:
    73	                celestrak_context = (
    74	                    f"\n\nCelesTrak orbital data for NORAD {norad_id}:\n"
    75	                    f"  Name: {sat_data['name']}\n"
    76	                    f"  COSPAR ID: {sat_data['cospar_id']}\n"
    77	                    f"  Orbital regime: {sat_data['orbital_regime']}\n"
    78	                    f"  Altitude: {sat_data['altitude_avg_km']} km\n"
    79	                    f"  Inclination: {sat_data['inclination_deg']}°\n"
    80	                    f"  Launch date: {sat_data['launch_date']}\n"
    81	                    f"  Country: {sat_data['country_code']}\n"
    82	                    f"  RCS size: {sat_data['rcs_size']}"
    83	                )
    84	        except Exception as e:
    85	            log.warning("CelesTrak lookup failed", exc_info=True)
    86	
    87	    prompt = f"Classify this satellite image.{celestrak_context}"

    90	
    91	    agent = _get_agent()
    92	
    93	    try:
    94	        data = await run_adk_agent(
    95	            agent,
    96	            prompt,
    97	            image_bytes=image_bytes,
    98	            image_mime=image_mime,
    99	        ) if agent else await _fallback(prompt, image_bytes, image_mime)
   100	
   101	        # Fail-closed: reject unparseable agent responses
   102	        if "error" in data and "raw_text" in data:
   103	            log.warning("Classification returned unparseable response")
   104	            return ClassificationResult(
   105	                valid=False,
   106	                rejection_reason="Agent response could not be parsed",
   107	                degraded=True,
   108	            )
   109	
   110	        return ClassificationResult(**data)
   111	    except Exception as e:
   112	        log.error("Classification failed", exc_info=True)
   113	        return ClassificationResult(
   114	            valid=False,
   115	            rejection_reason="Classification unavailable: agent error",
   116	            satellite_type="other",
   117	            orbital_regime="UNKNOWN",
   118	            notes=f"Classification failed: {e}",
   119	            degraded=True,
   120	        )

   122	
   123	async def _fallback(prompt: str, image_bytes: bytes, image_mime: str) -> dict:

   132	                role="user",
   133	                parts=[
   134	                    types.Part.from_text(text=_PROMPT_TEMPLATE + "\n\n" + prompt),
   135	                    types.Part.from_bytes(data=image_bytes, mime_type=image_mime),
   136	                ],
   137	            ),
   138	            config=types.GenerateContentConfig(
   139	                response_mime_type="application/json",
   140	                temperature=0.1,

# Codex GPT-5.4 Audit of Claude's Karpathy-Strategy Analysis
## Date: 2026-04-19
## Subject: /tmp/claude-analysis-2026-04-19.md (Claude Opus 4.7)

## Dimension Scores
| # | Dimension | Score | Evidence |
|---|-----------|-------|----------|
| D1 | First-principles rigor | 5/10 | Strong on thin-slice and governance boundaries, weak on separating necessity from preference. Claude treats two tables, a five-key index, universal falsifiers, fixed cadences, and deterministic crystallization as hard constraints (`/tmp/claude-analysis-2026-04-19.md:21-47`) when the memo supports less rigid but still viable variants (`ops/architecture/KARPATHY_LLM_WIKI_STRATEGY.md:331-366,425-451,705-727`). |
| D2 | Factual accuracy against repo | 6/10 | Evidence lineage is real (`backend/db/models.py:180-237`; `backend/services/evidence_ingest_service.py:53-90`; `backend/services/post_analysis_service.py:268-330`), but provenance is only a partial scaffold (`backend/models/provenance.py:20-35`; `backend/models/satellite.py:213-222`; `backend/agents/insurance_risk_agent.py:160-213`) and fail-closed behavior is split across orchestrator/governance/decision policy, not resident in `decision_policy_service.py` alone (`backend/agents/orchestrator.py:254-287`; `backend/services/governance_service.py:21-60`; `backend/services/decision_policy_service.py:86-183`). |
| D3 | Governance / safety | 4/10 | Two tables plus promotion API help, but Claude never ties them to the real enforcement point: persisted context-pack filtering and audit of injected memory. `decision_policy_service.py` never sees claim provenance (`backend/services/decision_policy_service.py:86-183`); the memo’s `context_packs` are the stronger control surface (`ops/architecture/KARPATHY_LLM_WIKI_STRATEGY.md:341-343,411-423,620-625`). |
| D4 | Security | 3/10 | Claude notices public-data corroboration (`/tmp/claude-analysis-2026-04-19.md:31-32`) but misses model drift/pinning (`backend/config.py:17-18`; `backend/services/governance_service.py:12-18`), permissive JSON extraction (`backend/services/gemini_service.py:104-121`), stored prompt injection via user/baseline text (`backend/agents/orbital_classification_agent.py:87-89`; `backend/main.py:300-304,410-427`), tenant/classification bleed (`ops/architecture/KARPATHY_LLM_WIKI_STRATEGY.md:541-548,721-727,789`), and the repo’s prior offline-eval leak class (`backend/tests/test_offline_eval.py:190-216,332-363`). |
| D5 | Completeness vs memo | 4/10 | Claude under-engages with memo strengths already present: DB-first claims (`ops/architecture/KARPATHY_LLM_WIKI_STRATEGY.md:522-529`), persisted context packs (`ops/architecture/KARPATHY_LLM_WIKI_STRATEGY.md:411-423,620-625`), runtime-eligibility/review states (`ops/architecture/KARPATHY_LLM_WIKI_STRATEGY.md:356-366,429-452,656-674`), and decay/expiry (`ops/architecture/KARPATHY_LLM_WIKI_STRATEGY.md:705-709`). |
| D6 | 30-day plan realism | 3/10 | Current `test_offline_eval.py` is dataset registry plus leak-guardrail scaffolding, not precedent/context-pack uplift measurement (`backend/tests/test_offline_eval.py:1-10,46-512`). Claude’s Days 1-5 plan requires new harnesses and 10/20 hand-authored packs (`/tmp/claude-analysis-2026-04-19.md:42-47,59-62`), which is both optimistic and internally inconsistent. |

## Critical Findings

### S1. Claude overstates the memo’s build-before-measure flaw
Claim under review: eval must precede even minimal thin-slice build.  
Quote: "Phase 3 (Prove Uplift) comes after 6-10 days of Phase 1-2 build."  
Evidence: Claude is right that the memo defers uplift proof to Phase 3 (`ops/architecture/KARPATHY_LLM_WIKI_STRATEGY.md:636-655`). He ignores that Phase 0 already defines success before build (`ops/architecture/KARPATHY_LLM_WIKI_STRATEGY.md:572-594`), and the memo’s eval is on system-produced case pages/context packs, not hand-written substitutes. The repo also has no existing precedent-eval harness to simply turn on (`backend/tests/test_offline_eval.py:1-10,46-512`).  
Verdict: modify.

### S1. "Table boundaries, not column boundaries" is asserted as necessity, not proved
Claim under review: a two-table lifecycle is the required governance mechanism.  
Quote: "`runtime_eligible: bool` as column — correct concept, wrong mechanism. Governance invariants belong at table boundaries, not column boundaries."  
Evidence: The need for explicit runtime eligibility and review is real (`ops/architecture/KARPATHY_LLM_WIKI_STRATEGY.md:356-366,429-452`). But the current fail-closed path lives in prompt-time evidence-gap handling and post-run governance, not in schema shape (`backend/agents/orchestrator.py:254-287`; `backend/services/governance_service.py:21-60`; `backend/services/decision_policy_service.py:127-183`). Without persisted context-pack provenance (`ops/architecture/KARPATHY_LLM_WIKI_STRATEGY.md:411-423,620-625`), two tables alone do not stop unsafe memory from reaching the prompt.  
Verdict: overturn.

### S2. Claude credits the repo with more provenance discipline than it actually has
Claim under review: the repo already has a strong typed/provenance worldview.  
Quote: "`backend/models/evidence.py and provenance.py already encode a typed world.`"  
Evidence: Typed evidence enums and bundles do exist (`backend/models/evidence.py:15-90`). But `FieldProvenance` is minimal and timestamp-free (`backend/models/provenance.py:20-25`), claim-level provenance fields on `InsuranceRiskReport` are optional (`backend/models/satellite.py:213-222`), and missing provenance is silently stubbed after LLM output (`backend/agents/insurance_risk_agent.py:160-213`). That is scaffolding, not a rigorous compiled-claim substrate.  
Verdict: modify.

### S2. Claude’s adversarial model is incomplete
Claim under review: cross-source corroboration is the missing security spine.  
Quote: "Public-data-derived claims ... require cross-source corroboration from ≥2 independent sources before runtime eligibility."  
Evidence: Corroboration is sensible for some public-derived claims. It is not the full threat model. Claude omits model drift and weak pinning (`backend/config.py:17-18`; `backend/services/governance_service.py:12-18`), permissive JSON salvage (`backend/services/gemini_service.py:104-121`), stored prompt injection via `additional_context` and future compiled markdown (`backend/agents/orbital_classification_agent.py:87-89`; `backend/main.py:300-304,410-427`), tenant/classification segregation (`ops/architecture/KARPATHY_LLM_WIKI_STRATEGY.md:541-548,721-727,789`), and the repo’s prior offline-eval bleed pattern (`backend/tests/test_offline_eval.py:190-216,332-363`).  
Verdict: overturn.

### S2. The Days 1-5 plan is optimistic relative to the actual scaffold
Claim under review: a five-day front-loaded eval phase is realistic.  
Quote: "Days 1-5: Eval harness. 20 precedent packs hand-written."  
Evidence: Reusable pieces exist only for dataset registration and runtime/offline separation (`backend/tests/test_offline_eval.py:46-274`). There is no existing harness for retrieval precision, citation precision, analyst agreement, or with/without context-pack delta (`backend/tests/test_offline_eval.py:1-10,281-512`). Claude is also inconsistent about scope: 10 hand-written packs at `/tmp/claude-analysis-2026-04-19.md:42`, 20 at `:59`.  
Verdict: overturn.

### S3. "Staleness is missing" overstates the memo’s gap
Claim under review: the memo lacks a staleness invariant.  
Quote: "Three first-class invariants are missing: falsifiability, staleness, and cross-source corroboration."  
Evidence: Claude is right that the memo does not define per-claim cadences or demotion mechanics. But the memo already includes retention/decay policies, class-relative decay, and explicit runtime-eligibility expiry (`ops/architecture/KARPATHY_LLM_WIKI_STRATEGY.md:356-366,705-709,748-750`). This is under-specified, not absent.  
Verdict: modify.

## Where Claude Is Actually Right
- The competing autonomous-intelligence-layer plan is too large for first proof: 31 new files, 3 migrations, and ~2,630 LOC before showing uplift (`brainstorming/autonomous-intelligence-layer-plan.md:293-324`) versus the memo’s thin-slice gate (`ops/architecture/KARPATHY_LLM_WIKI_STRATEGY.md:274-284,636-655`).
- Canonical claims should not live in markdown-as-truth; human-readable pages can be inspection artifacts, but governed runtime state belongs in the database (`ops/architecture/KARPATHY_LLM_WIKI_STRATEGY.md:522-529`).
- Any compiled memory that reaches runtime must remain subordinate to fail-closed governance and mandatory human review (`backend/agents/orchestrator.py:254-287`; `backend/services/governance_service.py:21-60`; `backend/services/decision_policy_service.py:171-183`).
- Structured filters and typed evidence should come before vector-heavy retrieval in this domain (`backend/models/evidence.py:15-90`; `ops/architecture/KARPATHY_LLM_WIKI_STRATEGY.md:550-559`).

## Where Claude Overclaims Hard-to-Vary Status
- `proposed_claims` plus `runtime_claims` as a mandatory table split. The invariant is controlled promotion plus auditable retrieval; schema split is one implementation choice, not physics (`/tmp/claude-analysis-2026-04-19.md:21`; `ops/architecture/KARPATHY_LLM_WIKI_STRATEGY.md:429-452,715-727`).
- Universal `falsifier` field. Valuable for hypotheses, not obviously required for catalog facts, reference profiles, or case-page summaries (`/tmp/claude-analysis-2026-04-19.md:26`; `backend/db/models.py:149-177`; `backend/services/post_analysis_service.py:99-250`).
- Fixed cadences `180d/30d/14d`. Sensible defaults, not hard-to-vary truths grounded in repo data (`/tmp/claude-analysis-2026-04-19.md:29`; `ops/architecture/KARPATHY_LLM_WIKI_STRATEGY.md:705-709`).
- Five-key case-page index. Retrieval heuristic, not necessity; the repo does not even normalize `failure_family` today (`/tmp/claude-analysis-2026-04-19.md:20,43`; `backend/models/satellite.py:149-160`).
- Deterministic pure-function crystallizer. Helpful for regression, but strict determinism is not the only safe path when vendor LLMs are configurable and drift-prone (`/tmp/claude-analysis-2026-04-19.md:45`; `backend/config.py:17-18`; `backend/services/gemini_service.py:55-57,104-121`).
- `>=15%` uplift as a kill threshold. Useful management heuristic, not first-principles necessity; the repo has no baseline establishing that cutoff (`/tmp/claude-analysis-2026-04-19.md:22`; `backend/tests/test_offline_eval.py:1-10`).
- "Context engineering beats prompt engineering" as a repo-grounded axiom. Directionally plausible, but Claude presents an industry belief as if it were project-specific proof (`/tmp/claude-analysis-2026-04-19.md:13`).

## Missing Counterarguments
- The memo already has staleness/decay/expiry; the right critique is "under-specified," not "missing" (`ops/architecture/KARPATHY_LLM_WIKI_STRATEGY.md:356-366,705-709`).
- The memo already preserves exact `context_packs` for audit and replay, which is a stronger safety control than Claude foregrounds (`ops/architecture/KARPATHY_LLM_WIKI_STRATEGY.md:411-423,620-625`).
- Hand-written packs validate analyst priors, but they do not test automated crystallization quality, which is the memo’s actual product risk (`ops/architecture/KARPATHY_LLM_WIKI_STRATEGY.md:595-655`).
- The memo explicitly keeps case pages first and claims later; Claude’s Day 6-20 plan pulls claim infrastructure forward faster than the memo does (`ops/architecture/KARPATHY_LLM_WIKI_STRATEGY.md:331-349,656-674`; `/tmp/claude-analysis-2026-04-19.md:60-61`).
- Blanket two-source promotion gates ignore source authority and claim class. Some single-source but authoritative or tenant-private facts can still be usable after review (`backend/services/evidence_service.py:137-171,255-291,303-327,334-375`).
- Claude should have addressed stored prompt injection, Gemini drift, tenant/classification scoping, and offline_eval leak reuse, not only public-data corroboration (`backend/agents/orbital_classification_agent.py:87-89`; `backend/services/gemini_service.py:104-121`; `backend/tests/test_offline_eval.py:190-216,332-363`; `ops/architecture/KARPATHY_LLM_WIKI_STRATEGY.md:541-548,721-727,789`).

## Dissent: Where Codex Disagrees with Claude
- I do not agree that two tables are the necessary governance boundary. I agree that promotion and retrieval must be gated.
- I do not agree that hand-authored packs should replace the memo’s minimal build-before-measure loop. They should at most supplement it.
- I do not agree that `provenance.py` proves the repo is already ready for claim-level compiled memory. It proves only that the team has a partial report-side provenance scaffold.
- I do not agree that `baseline_reference` is currently a live runtime bypass path. It is a future risk, not a present read path (`backend/main.py:300-304,410-427`; `backend/services/post_analysis_service.py:103-141,329-342`).

## Recommendations
1. Recast the verdict so `staleness` becomes `present but under-specified`, while falsifiability and adversarial promotion checks remain genuine additions. Value: High. Effort: Low.
2. Replace the two-table mandate with an enforcement-point analysis: promotion workflow, retrieval filter, persisted context-pack/source-hash manifest, and analysis audit fields. Value: High. Effort: Medium.
3. Downgrade "repo already has provenance worldview" to "partial scaffold" and cite the optional/stubbed reality in `provenance.py` and `insurance_risk_agent.py`. Value: High. Effort: Low.
4. Expand the security section to cover stored prompt injection, model drift/pinning, tenant/classification isolation, and reuse of the offline_eval leak lessons. Value: High. Effort: Medium.
5. Keep the memo’s product-path eval, but add a smaller manual preflight: 5 exemplar case pages/context packs, not 20, unless Claude also budgets time to build the missing harness. Value: High. Effort: Medium.
6. If Claude wants corroboration gates, scope them by claim class and source authority instead of a blanket `>=2` rule. Value: Medium. Effort: Medium.

## Attribution

# Codex GPT-5.4 Audit of Claude's Karpathy-Strategy Analysis
## Date: 2026-04-19
## Subject: /tmp/claude-analysis-2026-04-19.md (Claude Opus 4.7)

## Dimension Scores
| # | Dimension | Score | Evidence |
|---|-----------|-------|----------|
| D1 | First-principles rigor | 5/10 | Strong on thin-slice and governance boundaries, weak on separating necessity from preference. Claude treats two tables, a five-key index, universal falsifiers, fixed cadences, and deterministic crystallization as hard constraints (`/tmp/claude-analysis-2026-04-19.md:21-47`) when the memo supports less rigid but still viable variants (`ops/architecture/KARPATHY_LLM_WIKI_STRATEGY.md:331-366,425-451,705-727`). |
| D2 | Factual accuracy against repo | 6/10 | Evidence lineage is real (`backend/db/models.py:180-237`; `backend/services/evidence_ingest_service.py:53-90`; `backend/services/post_analysis_service.py:268-330`), but provenance is only a partial scaffold (`backend/models/provenance.py:20-35`; `backend/models/satellite.py:213-222`; `backend/agents/insurance_risk_agent.py:160-213`) and fail-closed behavior is split across orchestrator/governance/decision policy, not resident in `decision_policy_service.py` alone (`backend/agents/orchestrator.py:254-287`; `backend/services/governance_service.py:21-60`; `backend/services/decision_policy_service.py:86-183`). |
| D3 | Governance / safety | 4/10 | Two tables plus promotion API help, but Claude never ties them to the real enforcement point: persisted context-pack filtering and audit of injected memory. `decision_policy_service.py` never sees claim provenance (`backend/services/decision_policy_service.py:86-183`); the memo’s `context_packs` are the stronger control surface (`ops/architecture/KARPATHY_LLM_WIKI_STRATEGY.md:341-343,411-423,620-625`). |
| D4 | Security | 3/10 | Claude notices public-data corroboration (`/tmp/claude-analysis-2026-04-19.md:31-32`) but misses model drift/pinning (`backend/config.py:17-18`; `backend/services/governance_service.py:12-18`), permissive JSON extraction (`backend/services/gemini_service.py:104-121`), stored prompt injection via user/baseline text (`backend/agents/orbital_classification_agent.py:87-89`; `backend/main.py:300-304,410-427`), tenant/classification bleed (`ops/architecture/KARPATHY_LLM_WIKI_STRATEGY.md:541-548,721-727,789`), and the repo’s prior offline-eval leak class (`backend/tests/test_offline_eval.py:190-216,332-363`). |
| D5 | Completeness vs memo | 4/10 | Claude under-engages with memo strengths already present: DB-first claims (`ops/architecture/KARPATHY_LLM_WIKI_STRATEGY.md:522-529`), persisted context packs (`ops/architecture/KARPATHY_LLM_WIKI_STRATEGY.md:411-423,620-625`), runtime-eligibility/review states (`ops/architecture/KARPATHY_LLM_WIKI_STRATEGY.md:356-366,429-452,656-674`), and decay/expiry (`ops/architecture/KARPATHY_LLM_WIKI_STRATEGY.md:705-709`). |
| D6 | 30-day plan realism | 3/10 | Current `test_offline_eval.py` is dataset registry plus leak-guardrail scaffolding, not precedent/context-pack uplift measurement (`backend/tests/test_offline_eval.py:1-10,46-512`). Claude’s Days 1-5 plan requires new harnesses and 10/20 hand-authored packs (`/tmp/claude-analysis-2026-04-19.md:42-47,59-62`), which is both optimistic and internally inconsistent. |

## Critical Findings

### S1. Claude overstates the memo’s build-before-measure flaw
Claim under review: eval must precede even minimal thin-slice build.  
Quote: "Phase 3 (Prove Uplift) comes after 6-10 days of Phase 1-2 build."  
Evidence: Claude is right that the memo defers uplift proof to Phase 3 (`ops/architecture/KARPATHY_LLM_WIKI_STRATEGY.md:636-655`). He ignores that Phase 0 already defines success before build (`ops/architecture/KARPATHY_LLM_WIKI_STRATEGY.md:572-594`), and the memo’s eval is on system-produced case pages/context packs, not hand-written substitutes. The repo also has no existing precedent-eval harness to simply turn on (`backend/tests/test_offline_eval.py:1-10,46-512`).  
Verdict: modify.

### S1. "Table boundaries, not column boundaries" is asserted as necessity, not proved
Claim under review: a two-table lifecycle is the required governance mechanism.  
Quote: "`runtime_eligible: bool` as column — correct concept, wrong mechanism. Governance invariants belong at table boundaries, not column boundaries."  
Evidence: The need for explicit runtime eligibility and review is real (`ops/architecture/KARPATHY_LLM_WIKI_STRATEGY.md:356-366,429-452`). But the current fail-closed path lives in prompt-time evidence-gap handling and post-run governance, not in schema shape (`backend/agents/orchestrator.py:254-287`; `backend/services/governance_service.py:21-60`; `backend/services/decision_policy_service.py:127-183`). Without persisted context-pack provenance (`ops/architecture/KARPATHY_LLM_WIKI_STRATEGY.md:411-423,620-625`), two tables alone do not stop unsafe memory from reaching the prompt.  
Verdict: overturn.

### S2. Claude credits the repo with more provenance discipline than it actually has
Claim under review: the repo already has a strong typed/provenance worldview.  
Quote: "`backend/models/evidence.py and provenance.py already encode a typed world.`"  
Evidence: Typed evidence enums and bundles do exist (`backend/models/evidence.py:15-90`). But `FieldProvenance` is minimal and timestamp-free (`backend/models/provenance.py:20-25`), claim-level provenance fields on `InsuranceRiskReport` are optional (`backend/models/satellite.py:213-222`), and missing provenance is silently stubbed after LLM output (`backend/agents/insurance_risk_agent.py:160-213`). That is scaffolding, not a rigorous compiled-claim substrate.  
Verdict: modify.

### S2. Claude’s adversarial model is incomplete
Claim under review: cross-source corroboration is the missing security spine.  
Quote: "Public-data-derived claims ... require cross-source corroboration from ≥2 independent sources before runtime eligibility."  
Evidence: Corroboration is sensible for some public-derived claims. It is not the full threat model. Claude omits model drift and weak pinning (`backend/config.py:17-18`; `backend/services/governance_service.py:12-18`), permissive JSON salvage (`backend/services/gemini_service.py:104-121`), stored prompt injection via `additional_context` and future compiled markdown (`backend/agents/orbital_classification_agent.py:87-89`; `backend/main.py:300-304,410-427`), tenant/classification segregation (`ops/architecture/KARPATHY_LLM_WIKI_STRATEGY.md:541-548,721-727,789`), and the repo’s prior offline-eval bleed pattern (`backend/tests/test_offline_eval.py:190-216,332-363`).  
Verdict: overturn.

### S2. The Days 1-5 plan is optimistic relative to the actual scaffold
Claim under review: a five-day front-loaded eval phase is realistic.  
Quote: "Days 1-5: Eval harness. 20 precedent packs hand-written."  
Evidence: Reusable pieces exist only for dataset registration and runtime/offline separation (`backend/tests/test_offline_eval.py:46-274`). There is no existing harness for retrieval precision, citation precision, analyst agreement, or with/without context-pack delta (`backend/tests/test_offline_eval.py:1-10,281-512`). Claude is also inconsistent about scope: 10 hand-written packs at `/tmp/claude-analysis-2026-04-19.md:42`, 20 at `:59`.  
Verdict: overturn.

### S3. "Staleness is missing" overstates the memo’s gap
Claim under review: the memo lacks a staleness invariant.  
Quote: "Three first-class invariants are missing: falsifiability, staleness, and cross-source corroboration."  
Evidence: Claude is right that the memo does not define per-claim cadences or demotion mechanics. But the memo already includes retention/decay policies, class-relative decay, and explicit runtime-eligibility expiry (`ops/architecture/KARPATHY_LLM_WIKI_STRATEGY.md:356-366,705-709,748-750`). This is under-specified, not absent.  
Verdict: modify.

## Where Claude Is Actually Right
- The competing autonomous-intelligence-layer plan is too large for first proof: 31 new files, 3 migrations, and ~2,630 LOC before showing uplift (`brainstorming/autonomous-intelligence-layer-plan.md:293-324`) versus the memo’s thin-slice gate (`ops/architecture/KARPATHY_LLM_WIKI_STRATEGY.md:274-284,636-655`).

1. Recast the verdict so `staleness` becomes `present but under-specified`, while falsifiability and adversarial promotion checks remain genuine additions. Value: High. Effort: Low.
